Tullianum, di Ruma... 
 
«Mamertine  Carcere  d  lêebs  yellan  ddaw  tmurt,  deg-s  sin 
wannagen.  Tama  n  wadda  d  tasraft,  isem-is  Tullianum. 
Tedrem,  yezzi-as-d  ugadir,  iqba  s  uéru.  Yiwen  yimi  si  tama 
ufella i d tawwurt-is, am zun d imi n wecbali. D amkan yexlan, 
yertem, yumes, yettulles, yessaggad». 
 

Sɣur Salluste

- 1 - 
Tazwart 

 
 
 
 
 

 
 

Di  1977  nni,  di  Paris,  i  yufiɣ  adlis  n  Salluste,  ṭṭṛad  n 
Yugurten/La  Guerre  de  Jugurtha  (Bellum  Yugurthinum),  di 
Librairie  Maspero.  Adlis-nni  ɣliɣ  fell-as  ur  bniɣ.  D  yiwen 
umeddakel  iyi-d-yennan  :  Atan  «Maspero  yeznuzu  idlisen  am 
zun  d  tikci,  akken  ad  yeqfel  taêanut-is  ussan-agi  d-iteddun. 
Llan din wid yelhan, azzel skud ur fuken !». 
Akken  i  tevṛa.  Ass-nni  kan  ufiɣ-d  iman-iw  di  têanut  n 
Maspero,  di  Quartier  latin,  xtareɣ-d  idlisen  ara  d-aɣeɣ.  Isem-
nni n Salluste, sliɣ yes-s zik, ur cfiɣ ma lliɣ sneɣ ayen yura neɣ 
ur t-ssineɣ. Salluste ilul di tmurt n Rruman deg useggas n -87. 
Yugurten  yemmut  di  -104.  Ger  tmettant  (lmut)  n  Yugurten 
akked  tlalit  n  Salluste  zrin  18  yiseggasen.  Mi  yura  Salluste 
adlis-nni «Bellum Yugurthinum» La Guerre de Jugurtha, ad yili 
di leâmer-is ger 30 d 40 yiseggasen. 
Nezmer  ad  nini  llan  kan  60  yiseggasen  ger  tmettant  n 
Yugurten  d  yeḍṛan  di  Yennayer  n  -104  akked  tira  n  udlis  n 
Salluste. Tallit n 60 yiseggasen amzun d ulac di tira n umezruy. 
Di  leqrun-nni,  tamurt  ur  tettbeddil  udem  di  60  yiseggasen, 
maççi am wass-a. 
Tira-nni n Salluste banent-iyi-d am zun d tamuɣli n win yellan 
dinna,  d  anagi  di  ṭṭṛad  n  Yugurten  mgal  Rruman.  Mi  bdiɣ 
adlis-nni, ufiɣ-t am zun d tawwurt i d-yeldin zdat-i i wakken  

                                                            

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

ad éreɣ amezruy n Yugurten, amezruy n Tmazɣa4. 
£as akken yeççur tiî, di tedyant-nni ufiɣ ixuû kra. Syin ɣer zdat, 
acêal n tikkal i ttalseɣ taɣuri i wedlis-nni. Yal aseggas ad t-id-
ddmeɣ,  ad  t-ɣreɣ  tikkelt  neɣ  snat,  sakin  ad  t-serseɣ.  Tuɣal-iyi 
am win itessen irennu-as fad. Yal tikkelt éerreɣ zdat wallen-iw 
agellid  Yugurten  iteddu,  yettazzal,  iferru  tilufa  n  tmurt-is, 
yekkat aneccab deg yimenɣi, iteddu ɣef ugmer deg uzaɣar neɣ 
deg  yidurar,  icudd  s  txelxalin  n  wuzzal...  Taggara,  ufiɣ  ayen 
ixuûûen deg udlis-nni : ixuûû wawal n Yugurten. 
Di 2006, di «La Foire du Livre» n Paris, i d-ɣliɣ tikkelt tis snat 
ɣef udlis5-nni n Salluste. Mi t-id-ddmeɣ, ufiɣ d adlis i d-yeffɣen 
di Lezzayer ɣur «Grand Alger Editions». Feṛêeɣ mi yufiɣ adlis-
nni. Feṛêeɣ ugar imi adlis d-iêekkun tudert n Yugurten yeffeɣ-
d di tmurt n Yugurten. Ass-nni tban-iyi-d Tmazɣa n Yugurten 
d Lezzayer n wass-a, yiwet n tmurt ! 
2112  yiseggasen  zrin  seg-mi  yemmut  Yugurten.  £as  netta 
yemmut, isem-is d ubrid d-yewwi ɣef tmurt-is, ar ass-a ddren. 
Abrid-is yenjer seg yiseggasen-nni n ṭṭrad mgal Rruman. 
Akken  ad  d-yuɣal  wawal  n  Yugurten,  ufiɣ  llan  sin  yiberdan  : 
asuqqel n udlis n Salluste s tmaziɣt, d ubrid wis sin. 
Asuqqel  n  udlis  kseɣ-t  si  tazwara.  Ufiɣ  asuqqel  n  udlis  d 
timerna kan ara rnuɣ awal i wawal n Salluste. Nekk ɣur-i, ufiɣ 
yezwar wawal n Yugurten. Asuqqel ad yas wass-is. 
Taggara, qqimeɣ-as, wwteɣ ad skefleɣ ayen izemren ad yili deg 
wallaɣ  n  Yugurten  di  tallit-nni  i  deg  yennuɣ  Rruman,  seg-mi 
tebda armi d asmi tewwev talast n ṭṭrad... 
Di yal tadyant d-yeêka Salluste6, wwteɣ ad afeɣ amek ara yegg 
yiwen yellan d Amaziɣ, zdat tlufa n yimir-nni. 
Di tira n Salluste llan sin wudmawen. Yiwen d udem n umaru 
d-iêekkun tadyant akken tella, akken i as-tt-id-êkan, akken i tt-
yeɣra deg yedlisen yellan imir-nni. Wis sin d udem n Uṛumani 

                                                            
4  Tamazɣa  tella  tebva  ɣef  sin  :  Tamazɣa  n  ugmuv  (Tunes  d  ugmuv  n  Lezzayer), 
Tamazɣa n utaram (Merruk d umur n utaram n Lezzayer). Akin tella Libya d Tniri 
(ṣṣeêṛa). 
5 La Guerre de Jugurtha. Editions GAL / Grand Alger Editions, 2005. 
6 Salluste yeêka-d amur ameqqran seg wayen yeɣra deg yidlisen yura C. Sulla, win 
d-yeîîfen Yugurten d ameêbus di taggara n useggas -105. 

- 10 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

n  Ruma,  win  iéerren  s  tiî  n  weɣref  iêekmen  ddunit  imir-nni. 
Yella deg wawal : «Ruma i d-yekkan nnig tmura» ! 
Ma yella wugur gar sin yexûimen, anda yella lkil, yal yiwen ad 
d-yeêku tadyant-is akken tella. Win d amennuɣ n yizmawen ; 
dinna  i  tferru  s  lêeqq.  Deg  udlis  n  Salluste,  di  yiwet  tedyant 
kan  i  d-yeggra  wawal  n  Yugurten,  d  awal-nni  i  as-yenna  ass-
nni  i  deg  d-yeffeɣ  s  wurfan  si  teɣremt  n  Ruma,  yenna-as  deg 
wawal-is7 : «Tiɣremt usekkak, ad yas wass n nnger-is asmi ara 
taf bab-is» / Vrbem uenalem et mature perituram si emptorem 
inuenerit. 
Tawaɣit,  ɣas  d  awal  n  Yugurten  s  tidet,  d  awal  i  d-yenna  s 
trumanit  maççi  s  tmaziɣt  !  Awal-agi  n  Yugurten  i  d-yeggran 
ass-a, nezmer ad nini yecba awal-nni n jeddi-s, Masensen, asmi 
i  as-yenna  :  «Taferka  i  tarwa  n  tferka  !»  (L'Afrique  aux 
africains!). 
Deg usaru i aɣ-d-yeooa Salluste, nekni nerra awal n Iugurthae8 
i Yugurten n At Yiles. D netta i d-yiêekkun tadyant akken tella, 
neɣ akken «tezmer ad tili imir-nni». Di yal tadyant, newwet ad 
naf  awalen  yezmer  ad  yessiwel  Yugurten.  Nesdukel  asaru-nni 
n Salluste akked wawal n Yugurten i wakken ad myefken tayet, 
ad  aɣ-d-ssefflen  tafat  ɣef  leqrun-nni  imezwura  n  tmurt-nneɣ. 
£as adlis d ungal kan, ur yelli d adlis n umezruy. 
Di yal tadyant, di tallit n ṭṭṛad, neqqim kan deg udlis n Salluste. 
Ur  d-nerni  tadyant,  ur  nekkis.  Ayen  i  nekkes,  d  ayen  kan  d-
yenna Salluste ɣef tmeddurt akked tlufa n Rruman gar-asen.  
Taggara,  tanemmirt  tameqqrant  i  Salluste  i  aɣ-d-yeooan  tira 
tinigit, tira yeddren ɣef Yugurten9, ɣef umezruy n yimezwura-

                                                            

8 Iugurthae = Yugurten (Isem, akken t-yura Salluste s tlatinit). 
9  Awal  n  Salluste  ɣef  Yugurten  :  "...  Mi  yekker  Yugurten,  yuɣal  d  ileméi,  yesdukel 
tezyen, tirkelt akk d tegzi (tamussni). Yerna awal aéidan. Yekka-d nnig tezyiwin-is. 
Ur yeooa iman-is di tmeddurt n tinefcect n tarwa igelliden. Iteddu, yettazzal netta d 
yimeddukal-is, yekkat aneccab, acangal, irekkeb agmer am nepa am at tmurt-is. £as 
d  netta  i  d  amezwaru  di  yal  timsizzelt,  êemmlent  akk  wid  i  t-yesnen.  Yella  di  yal 
ûyada  n  yizem  di  téegwa  n  Tmazɣa.  Di  yal  tadyant,  netta  seg  yimezwura  i  tyita 

- 11 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

nneɣ.  Adlis  n  Salluste  yeldi-aɣ-d  tawwurt  ɣef  tallit  yezrin10, 
neéra  amur  di  tmeddurt  n  Yugurten  akked  watmaten-is  di 
twizi-nni  tameqqrant,  deg  yiseggasen-nni  uɣilif,  iseggasen  n 
yimeîîawen, n tidi d yidammen. 
Akken  yebɣu  yili  udlis,  akken  yebɣu  yerra-d  tadyant  am  zun 
tedder,  akken  tella,  yezmer  yiwen  ad  iéer  ayen  yellan  zdat 
wallen-is,  taggara,  adlis  yeqqim  d  awalen  kan.  D  awalen 
yesnin, d ayen ur yeîîif, ur yennul ufus. 
Di  ṭṭṛad  n  Yugurten,  imukan-nni  akk  seg  yekka  ugellid 
Yugurten, anda yuzzel, anda yennuɣ, anda yevsa, anda yeɣli… 
amur  ameqqran  deg-sen  llan,  ddren  ar  ass-a,  maççi  d 
tamacahut : Sirta, Zama, Carthage, Gafsa, Tuga, Tala, Campus 
Martius,  Via  Sacra,  Circus  Maximus,  Curia  (n  Senat), 
Capitolinus, ... Tullianum. 
Yugurten yemmut di tesraft n Tullianum di Ruma. Yemmut si 6 
wussan n laé d usemmiv. 
Mi  ara  nger  tamawt  i  tmeddurt  n  Yugurten,  tameddurt  n 
ukessar d usawen n wacêal d aseggas, ad naff tidet taqerêant : 
maççi  d  Rruman  i  t-yeṣṣawven  ɣer  tesraft  n  Tullianum.  D 
atmaten-is i t-yeskecmen. Iṛumaniyen ur as-zmiren di ṭṭṛad, ur 
as-zmiren  di  tiêḥeôci.  Ufan-as  kan 
iɣisi  di  tixubbta  n 
watmaten-is akk d idammen-is. 
Amezwaru  d  Hiemsal,  yessaɣ  times  tamezwarut  n  cwal, 
yewwet  ad  yekkes  Yugurten.  Aderbal  yeṣṣawev  tamsalt  armi 
yebva Tamazɣa ɣef sin, tamurt- nni n Masensen. 

                                                                                                                                
uneccab. Akken yella d amezwaru i tyita, i yella d aneggaru deg wawal ɣef yiman-
is..."Ïṭṛad n Yugurten, t. 11. 
10 Tadyant n Yugurten : Mi yemmut Masensen n at Yiles di -148, agellid n Tmazɣa 
(Numidya),  yuɣal  mmi-s  Makawsen  d  agellid.  Mi  yemmut  Makawsen  di  -118, 
yeooa-d  lwert  i  sin  warraw-is,  Aderbal  akk  d  Hiemsal,  akk  d  Yugurten,  mmi-s  n 
gma-s  Mastanabal.  Di  tazwara  kan  yewwet  yiɣisi  gar-asen.  Aseggas  amezwaru, 
Hiemsal  yemmut  deg  yimenɣi,  neɣ  seg  ufus  n  Yugurten  (?).  Aderbal  yekker-d  d 
axûim n Yugurten, yessuter i Yiṛumaniyen, bvan-asen tamurt ɣef sin yeêricen. Sirta 
tedda  deg  umur  n  Aderbal.  Si  -118  armi  d  -112  teqqim  akken.  Di  -112  tekker. 
Yugurten yezzi i Sirta, yekcem s lâesker-is, yeîîef Aderbal, yenɣa-t. Imir Ruma tuɣal 
d  nettat  i  d  taxûimt  n  Yugurten.  7  yiseggasen  n  yimenɣi  ger  Yugurten  akk  d 
Yirumaniyen. Di taggara n -105, gan-as ticeôket s ufus n ugellid Buxuc. Qqnen-as 
snasel,  wwin-t  ɣer  teɣremt  n  Ruma.  Yemmut  di  tesraft  n  Tullianum  di  yennayer  -
104, deffir 6 wussan n laé d usemmiv. 

- 12 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Masiwen,  yerna-d  tilufa-s,  deffir  tedyant  n  Aderbal,  akken  ad 
yebvu  tamurt  ula  d  netta ;  ad  yeddem  amur  n  Aderbal 
yemmuten. 
Gawda, yedda d axabit netta d yemnayen n Marius, yekker ad 
ineɣ  atmaten-is  Imaziɣen ;  yekker  ad  yeṣṣerɣ  tuddar  akk  d 
yigran. 
Jiniral Bumelxir, ameqqran n lâesker Amaziɣ, yekka-as si deffir 
i Yugurten, akken ad t-yezzenz i jiniral Metellus. 
Aneggaru  d  agellid  Buxus,  avewwal-is,  yefka-as 
tiyita 
taneggarut.  Yezzenz-it  i  Ruma  akken  ad  yessemɣer  akal-is. 
Afus, s tidet, deg-neɣ i yella. 
Akken  ad  éreɣ  s  wallen-iw  amkan  deg  yemmut  Yugurten,  ad 
beddeɣ anda ibedd, ad nnaleɣ s ufus-iw iéra-nni yennul s ufus-
is netta, riɣ ad kecmeɣ tiɣremt n Ruma. Riɣ ad awveɣ amkan-
nni. £as tiɣremt n Ruma ériɣ  tbeddel, Tullianum ur ibeddel si 
leqrun-nni imezwura. 
£as  amkan-nni  si  tama  ufella  ibeddel,  bnan-as  tamesgida  i 
téallit  di  leqrun  imezwura,  tasraft  akken  tella  i  d-teggra.  D 
awal  d-nnan  akk  wid  i  kecmen  amkan-nni.  Iéra-nni  d  wid 
yellan ass-nni i yellan ass-a. Riɣ ad ten-id-zureɣ. 
Acêal  n  wagguren  aya  seg-mi  tt-friɣ  d  yiman-iw,  ad  kecmeɣ 
Ruma.  Ussan  teddun,  aggur  deffir  wayev,  ass  n  tikli  ur  d 
yewwiv.  Ukiɣ  d  yiman-iw,  akken  riɣ  ad  kecmeɣ  amkan-nni  i 
yas-tezziɣ  i  wass  n  tikli.  Yal  tikkelt  yella  wayen  d-yettasen  d 
ugur i terzeft ɣer Ruma. 
Tikwal,  nekk  s  timmad-iw  teggeɣ  ccek  :  "s  tidet  mazal-it 
wemkan-nni  akken  i  t-id-yeooa  Yugurten  ?  Amek  yedrem ? 
Amek  yeḍyeq  ?  Amek  yettulles ?  Amek  yeqqim  Yugurten  ɣef 
yeéra-nni  ?  Amek  yella  usemmiv-is  di  tegrest  n  Ruma  ?  Yella 
wayen i umi isel mi yella dinna neɣ d tasusmi n tesraft-nni kan 
?  Yella  win  ikecmen  ɣur-s  yessawel  yid-s,  yenna-as  awal  neɣ 
sin,  yefka-as  ad  isew,  yefka-as  ad  yeçç?  I  Marius,  i  Sulla,  i 
yimeddukal-is  di  Ruma,  nudan  ad  éren  tawaɣit  deg  yella  ? 
Amek ? Amek ? 
Riɣ  ad  éreɣ  ayen  yella  yettḥulfu  yes-s  Yugurten  imir-nni,  mi 
tegren  seg  yimi  n  tesraft,  ooan-t  yenîeô  akessar,  yeɣli  am 
ucettiv deg tesraft n war tawwurt. 

- 13 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Yugurten yella yessen tiɣremt n Ruma seg yixef ɣer yixef. 
Yessen tizerbatin-is, yessen abrid n Curia, tazeqqa deg yettɣimi 
Senat,  yessen  daɣ  isem  n  wemkan-nni  deg  d-yeggra  ass-a : 
Mamertinum  d  Tullianum.  Yeéra  anta  i  d  taggara  n  wid 
ikecmen tasraft-nni. 
Di  tubeô  2008,  rziɣ  ɣer  teɣremt  n  Ruma.  Mi  kecmeɣ  ɣer 
tesraft-nni, rgagiɣ. Ukiɣ-as i uɣilif-nni ameqqran. 
I  tesraft  n  war  tawwurt,  ass-a  bnan-as  tiseddaôin  akken  ad 
kecmen ɣer-s yemzuṛen. D iéra-nni i yellan imir i yellan ass-a ; 
d tillas-nni i yellan imir i yellan ass-a. Kecmeɣ, serseɣ afus-iw 
ɣef yiran-nni n yimi n tesraft, imi-nni seg yenîer Yugurten ɣef 
yeblaven iṣemmaven.  Amkan-nni seg-s ur d yeffiɣ d ameddur. 
Nella  nbedd  di  tesraft-nni,  nekk  akk  d  warraw-iw,  nessusem, 
mi aɣ-d-tekcem terbaât n yemzuôen n Iṭalyaniyen neɣ wis anta 
tamurt.  Gar-asen  yella  wemnir,  « le  guide »  Aṭalyani,  i  sen-d-
yessefhamen amezruy n wemkan-nni. 
Mi aɣ-d-yesla nesawal s tmaziɣt, nekk akk d warraw-iw, yekfa 
awal-is  i  yemzuôen-nni,  dɣa  yezzi-d  ɣur-neɣ,  yenna-yaɣ-d  s 
tefôansist : 
-  Dagi  i  yemmut  ugellid  Yugurten,  agellid  ameqqran  n 
Numidya.  Aggur  agi  yezrin,  wwiɣ-d  ɣer  dagi  yiwet  n 
tamaziɣt  n  Lezzayer.  Asmi  d-tekcem 
tmeddakelt-iw,  d 
Tullianum,  tegumma  ad  tekfu  imeîîawen…  Yugurten  d  jedd-
is ! 
Nniɣ-as  i wemdan-nni : 
-  D  amezruy-nneɣ,  necrek-it,  nekni  akk  d  kenwi.  Ur  tella 
tuzzma ɣef leqrun d yiseggasen yezrin ! 
 
 
 
 

- 14 - 

 

 
 
 
 
 

- 2 - 
Ïṛad n Yugurten 

 
 
Deffir tallit n Makawsen11 

 
Seg  wass-mi  yemmut  wemɣar,  agellid  Makawsen, 
babat-nneɣ,  tamurt  ur  as-tufa  ixef-is.  Nekk  nwiɣ  imir  ibeddel 
wass, ad as- neqqim akken ad nbedd i tmurt-nneɣ. Mi yemmut 
babat-nneɣ, afud d nekni, ad as-neddukel i tcemlit tameqqrant. 
Am nekk, Aderbal akk d Hiemsal, ad nesdukkel tidi-nneɣ akken 
Tamazɣa ad as-nbeddel udem. 
Di  tazwara,  riɣ  ad  nekkes  tuqqna-nni  neqqen  ɣer  tmurt  n 
Rruman.  Nniɣ-asen  i  watmaten-iw,  ilaq-aɣ  ad  nerr  tilisa  n 
tmurt  seg  wanda  llant  zik.  Ad  nekkes  ugzir,  ad  nṣeggem 
tamurt-nneɣ. Ad neg iberdan, ad nessemɣer igran akk d tliwa n 
waman di yal tiɣremt, di yal tama n tmurt.  Ad nesbedd tiseɣlit 
i tlisa n tmurt akken yal Amaziɣ ad yaf iman-is yella deg wakal 
is.  Yiwen  weɣbel  ameqqran  i  yellan  zik,  ass-a  yekkes,  d 
Carthage  nni  i  aɣ-d-yellan  am  timmist  deg  wammas  acêal  d 
lqern, acêal d aseggas. Di tallit-nni, jedd-i, Masensen yeddukel 
netta  d  Rruman,  zzin-as  i  Carthage,  snegren-tt.  Tefra  tedyant-
nni, syin tuɣal-d akken tella. Di ṭṭṛad aneggaru mgal Carthage 
d  agellid  Makawsen  i  tuɣ  dinna.  D  imenɣi  aneggaru,  armi 
terɣa  teɣremt    n  Carthage  i  d-ters  telwit.  £as  akken,    Rruman 
yessekcem  tuccar-is  di  tmurt-nneɣ.  Iɣil  n  Carthage  yeôôeé, 
Rruman yuɣ amkan-is. Ayen yellan d akal ger tlisa n Carthage,

iêella-t  Rruman i nitni, snulfan-d tamurt tamaynut: « tamurt n

Ass-mi  yemmut  ugellid  Makawsen,  tiî-iw  nekk,  ad  nekkes 
azaglu-nni  yellan  fell-aɣ  acêal  aya.  Skud  yella  Rruman  ɣer 
yidisan-nneɣ, ur tezmir ad ters fell-aɣ telwit. 
Di  30  yiseggasen  n  tgelda  n  Makawsen,  seg  wass-mi  yemmut 
Masensen,  yeɣli-d  wegris  ɣef  tmurt-nneɣ.  Kkes-d  imenɣi

i  d-yernan  akken  ad  yuɣal  wakal  n  Tmazɣa  i  warraw-is. 
Makawsen yeqqim kan di tlisa-s am zun d tamellalt mi ara ad 
teɣli.  Rruman  yecrew  akk  akal  yellan  yeîîef-it  Carthage,  ma  d 
Makawsen yessusem-asen, am zun maççi d akal-nneɣ ! 
Tasusmi  n  30  yiseggasen  maççi  d  tasusmi,  d  tiggugemt  neɣ  d 
tesmev n wul.

d amdan-nni i umi yekkes uvar neɣ ufus.

tagelda i twizi tameqqrant. Newôet aɣbel, aɣbel-nni ameqqran 
n tmurt ad t-nbib ɣef tuyat-nneɣ. 
Nnan yiwen ufus ur yekkat llir. D tidet. Tella tegmat akken ad

Talast i yellan gar-i akk d Aderbal d Hiemsal d wa : nekk éerreɣ  
abrid-nni n jedd-i Masensen, "Taferka i tarwa n Tferka"14, ma d  
Hiemsal  akk  d  Aderbal  kksen  tamurt-nsen  ger  ifassen-nsen, 
kksen tamurt n Yimaziɣen i tarwa-s, fkan-tt d tarzeft i Rruman. 
Asmi  tekker  gar-aneɣ,  ṣṣawḍen-iyi-d  awalen  yenna  Uderbal 
dinna di Curia15 n Senat, tajmaât n Ruma, ass-mi yerwel akken 
ad yeccetki.  
Aderbal yenna-yas : 
"...Ass-mi  qrib  ad  yemmet  baba,  Makawsen,  yenna-i16 : 
"tamurt-a,  tagelda  n  Tmazɣa,  nekni  d  iqeddacen-is  kan. 
Imawlan-is n tidet d Rruman. Ilaq ad tgev ayen i umi tzemrev 
akken ad tallev aɣref n Rruman, am zun d idammen-ik". 
Am  zun  ur  yessuget  awal,  Aderbal  yerna  ugar  di  tebôat-nni 
yura  i  Rruman  ass-mi  i  as-nezzi  i  teɣremt  n  Sirta.  Aderbal 
yenna di tebrat-nni17 : "...Tagelda n Numidya-nwen kenwi, get- 
as  akken  tram,  kkset-iyi  kan  si  ger  tuccar  n  Yugurten  ;  di 
laânaya-nwen, di laânaya n tgelda n Rruman, i wudem n jedd-i 
Masensen...". 
Win  ara  yessiwven  taêilet  ɣer  talast  am  tagi,  ur  as-d-yegri 
yiseɣ, ur as-d-yeqqim yisem n tissas akken ad yili n uéar n At 
Yiles,  neɣ  ad  yeqqim  d  agellid  n  Tmazɣa.  Awalen-nni  yenna, 
asmi  i  asen-sliɣ,  tuli-yi-d  tkuffirt  seg  yedmaren-iw,  ukiɣ-as  i 
tkurt-nni  tcudd  turin-iw.  Aderbal  yekkes  abernus-is,  yeooa 
iman-is akken d aâeryan. Taggara, ur as-d-yegri yisem n yiseɣ. 
Ur yelli d gma. Idammen i d-aɣ-icerkan, nekk kkseɣ-ten akin. 
5 wagguren i as-nezzi s lâeskeô i teɣremt n Sirta. Taggara, tefra 
temsalt-is. Aderbal yuɣ abrid n Hiemsal, yemmut ula d netta.

D abrid i yuɣen i ten-yesnegren i sin18.

yeffeɣ-d  s  lâesker-is  ad  yeg  imenɣi.    Yettwaîîef,  yemmut  din 
zdat Sirta am netta am wid yellan yid-s.

Hiemsal  akk  d  Aderbal.  £as  d  gma  n  idammen,  yiwen  babat-
nneɣ, yiwen jedd-it-nneɣ Masensen, Masiwen ur d yeîîif anziz 
si tirrugza n jedd-is. Tamurt n baba-s d jedd-is yerra-tt d ayla n 
Rruman. Yebɣa ad d-yaɣ tagelda si Ruma. Masiwen yella dinna 
di Senat ger widen akken yessekren tiwuɣa. Yella ger wid-nni 
yessugguten aéeggi akk d tsusaf d yir awal ɣef Yugurten. 
Afus deg-neɣ i yella. 
Armi  tevra  twaɣit  i  fehmeɣ  anida  i  tella  twekka,  anida  i 
tesawev tyita. 
Iôumaniyen, tiêerci snen-as. Anda ur teîîif ad ndin tixfet anda 
nniven. D wid d-yesḥeṛcen Masiwen, zun d lexyal n tebêirt, i 
as-d-yefkan win  ara  s-yeqqimen. Fkan-as-t ad t-ineɣ akken ad 
smeɣren  taluft,  ad  awven  sanda  ssarmen :  anekcum  n 
Tamazɣa. 
Qqimen-as  i  Masiwen,  nɣan-t  di  tlemmast  n  Öuma.    Nitni 
nɣan-t, tiyita sbabben-tt i Bumelxiô,  nekk sefven-d ajenwi ɣer 
yiri-w. 
Ssuffɣen-d  awal,  yiwen  seg  wid-nni  yenɣan  yettwaîîef.  Nnan 
yudder-d  isem  n  Bumelxir  akk  d  Yugurten.  Di  herwel-nni, 
nniɣ-as i Bumelxir ad isenser iman-is si Ruma, tiêila n Rruman 
nessen-itent. Nniɣ-as netta ad yuɣal ɣer tmurt, nekk ad qqimeɣ 
ad  qableɣ  tajmaât  n  Senat.  Tundar-nsen  banent  am  uzal,  ala 
tasusmi i ur asen-ssusumeɣ ara. Akken teffeɣ teffeɣ. 
Nuɣal  ɣer  tejmaât  n  Senat.  Akken  nekcem  ɣer  Curia,  neqqim, 
dɣa  sekren  felli  ahlelli.  Ur  ooan  yir  awal,  ur  ooan  aéeggi.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Widen  yessazlen  idim  n  Masiwen  wwten  ad  glun  s  yixef-iw 
akken ad tt-frun di yiwet tegnit : nɣan Masiwen, akken ad glun 
s uqerruy n Yugurten. Ixef n tidet ur yella deg wawalen-nsen, 
awalen  n  times  n  Memmius.  D  tussda  kan  i  umi  d  stufan : 
« Amek ?  Tenɣiv  argaz  di  tlemmast  n  Ruma,  teréiv  laânaya  n 
tmurt-nneɣ ? Ur tgiv leqdeô i tmurt n Rruman !  Atg.... ».  
Ayen  akk  d-ssuffɣen,  nekk  ssusmeɣ,  gguniɣ  anda  ara  teffeɣ. 
àçiɣ s wallen widen d-yessawalen, yiwen yiwen akken ad cfuɣ 
fella-sen.  Win  ççiɣ  s  wallen  dɣa  netta  ad  isers  allen-is,  ad 
yessusem  am  zun  ur  yella  di  tirkeft-nni  n  yivan  yeseglafen. 
Zziɣ  tamuɣli-w  i  tzeqqa-nni  n  Senat.  èerreɣ  idurran-nni  n 
yemdanen. Nitni rekkmen seg wurfan, nekk rniɣ tasusmi, nitni 
rennun deg wurfan ugar. 
Taggara, mi kkreɣ ad neṭqeɣ, ad asen-iniɣ ayen riɣ, yesseɣl-iyi-
d  C.  Baebius,  yenna-yi-d :  « D  nekk  ara  yessiwlen,  keçç 
susem kan !».  Baebius  yessekfel-d  tiêila-nsen  yiwet  yiwet. 
Baebius  yefsi  tundar  i  cudden  s  wawalen  i  yes-s  tent-cudden 
nitni.  Yenna-yasen  tiqerêanin.  Taggara  yesseɣli-d  tasusmi, 
tiggugemt, di tejmaât n Senat. 
Yefra unejmaâ n Senat. Ticeôket-nsen tezgel. 
S  wurfan  n  taluft-nni  i  d-yernan  i  d-ffɣeɣ,  ooiɣ-en  Ruma  ɣer 
deffir, d abrid ɣer Sirîa. 
Tuffɣa  d-ffɣeɣ  si  Ruma,  fran-tt  nitni  ɣursen  zun  d  ansar  i  d-
nesreɣ,  d  tarewla  i  d-rewleɣ.  Wid  yundin  ticeôket-nni  ,  wid 
akken  yebɣan  ad  glun  s  uqerruy-iw,  ufan  tawwurt  i  seg  ara 
sseêmun  abendir  i  yat  Senat,  nnan :  «Mi  yerwel,  yuɣal  ɣer 
Numidya, d tidet, armi yenɣa !». Akka ! 
Di  Ruma  ggten  wid  yebɣan  cwal  ugar.  Mi  tent-xeôzen  akken 
Senat  ad  imil  ɣer  tama-nsen,  akken  ad  aɣ-yeîîef  akken  nella, 
taggara nniɣ-asen i yimeddukal-iw : ddut ! D abrid kan ara aɣ-
ijebôen. Ayen d yekkan gar-aɣ yid-sen drus ! 
Mi d neffeɣ si tiɣremt n Ruma, tuli-d tkurt n wurfan, zziɣ ɣer 
deffir, seɣleɣ ɣer teɣremt, dɣa nniɣ-asen : "Tiɣremt usekkak, ad 
d-yas wass n nger-is asmi ara taf bab-is".22

Mi d wwveɣ ɣer Tmazɣa, mi kecmeɣ Sirta i d-as-ukiɣ i twaɣit  
deg nella. Ayen akk nuzzel, taggara yenɣel, yewwi-t wasif.  
Aéar n tixubta yella deg-neɣ, taggara yerra-aɣ-tt-id akken tella 
di tazwara. Ad as-nuɣal i ugadir swadda. 
Di Sirta, giɣ aberraê, ɣreɣ i tejmaât n yemɣaren n tmurt. Usan 
d  akken  llan,  di  yal  tiɣmeôt  n  Tmazɣa,  di  yal  adrar,  di  yal 
azaɣar. Tadyant meqqret, iɣimi-s ad yiɣzif. 
Mi  tedduɣ  ad  asen-iniɣ  awalen  imezwura,  greɣ  tamawt  i 
tejmaât-nni, dɣa tkakiɣ d ayen ériɣ di tejmaât n Senat di Ruma, 
di Curia nni. 
Di Sirta ur llan at Nobilis, ur llan at popular. Yiwen wedrum i 
yellan. Zdat wallen-iw llan kan Imaziɣen am nekk. Yal yiwen d 
amɣar  n  tmurt  deg  yella,  yusa-d  seg  Wawras,  si  Weɣbalu,  si 
Tedmayt,  si  Tezmalt  neɣ  ansi  nniven.  Yal  yiwen  yusa-d  acku 
uznen-t-id  widen  yellan  dinna.  Ur  yelli  d  idammen  n  jedd-is, 
neɣ d igran n yirden-is i t-id-yessawven ɣer tejmaât n Tmazɣa 
di  Sirta.  èriɣ  imir  ayen  yellan  ɣur-neɣ,  ayen  ur  yellan  ɣur 
Rruman.  £ur-neɣ 
llant 
tseddaôin  gar  yemdanen.  Masensen,  jedd-i,  asmi  yuɣal  d 
agellid,  yuɣal  s  yiɣil-is  d  wayen  iga  s  timmad-is,  ur  yella  s 
idammen n jedd-is netta. 
Mi  neqqim,  wwiɣ-asen-d  i  wid  d  yezzin  tadyant  akken  tebda 
armi  d  taggara,  awal  zdat  Senat,  tixidas  n  wid  yebɣan  ad  aɣ-
snegren,  tadyant  n  Masiwen.    Nniɣ-asen  taggara,  ussan  d-
iteddun  ur  llan  d  ussan  n  tifrat  gar-aɣ  d  Rruman.  Si  tura,  ad 
nheggi iman-nneɣ i yimenɣi yid-sen. Tilisa-nneɣ d nekni kan i 
d  tiseɣlit-nsent.  Nniɣ-asen,  ma  zik  ngen  tanafa,  ass-a  ad  ngen 
kan  azgen,  ma  zik  neqqen  snat  wallen,  ass-a  ad  neqqen  kan 
yiwet tiî, ma zik nedda d tikli, ass-a ad nazzel. 
Nekk  sawleɣ-asen,  nitni  slan-d,  nnan-d  ayen  éran  d  abrid, 
tamuɣli-nneɣ yiwet. 
Tefra  tejmaât  n  yemɣaren,  tekker,  yal  yiwen  yuɣ  abrid-is  ad 
yeṣṣiwev  awal  i  yat  tmurt-is,  akken  ad  yesuffeɣ  aberraê 
ameqqran n tnekra.

Tallit n Albinus Postumius 

 
Bestia Calpurnius yezzi akin ɣer tmurt-is ur isers tifrat, 
ur  yeôéa  afud  n  Yugurten.  Awal-is  yeôéa-t  Senat  n  tmurt-is. 
Yuɣal ɣer Ruma am zun ur d yezgir. Di tegnit-nni, lâeskeô-nsen 
berken  di  tlisa  n  tmurt  n  Carthage,  nekni  nbedd  ɣef  yiman-
nneɣ, negguni ass-is. 
Ur negguni agguren mi nesla yezger-d jiniral Albinus s weglaf 
n lâeskeô.  Yal asafar n yimenɣi yegla-d yes-s. Acêal d ababuô i 
d-yeççuô akken ad yesemɣer ṭṭṛad. Yid-s yedda-d gma-s, Aulus, 
d  aâessekriw  am  netta.  Mi  aɣ-d-ṣṣawven  awal  wid  yellan  di 
Utique, di tmurt n Carthage, nekk suffɣeɣ awal i yal tamurt n 
Tmazɣa. Ass n ṭṭṛad ass-a yusa-d. 
Ussan imezwura, lâeskeô Iôumaniyen bdan ssuffuɣen-d tuccar-
nsen, tikwal da, tikwal din. Teddun am waôeẓéen-nni n teɣrast, 
ur  ooan  tiɣmert.  Yiwen  wass  ad  qqsen  tiɣremt,  igran,  ass 
nniven  ad  hudden  tiliwa  d  tmedwa  n  waman.  Ansi  kkan  d 
aɣilif,  ala  lmut,  idammen  akk  d  imeîîawen  i  d  ooaǧǧan  ɣer 
deffir.  Nitni  teddun,  nekni  tikwal  ngezzem-asen  abrid  a 
nemyewwat,  tikwal  neooa-ten  ad  zrin.  Tiî-nneɣ  nekni,  nebɣa 
ad  néer  amek  tikli-nsen.  Axbacen-nni-nsen,  iban-d  ur  yella  d 
abrid-nsen  nitni.  Iban  d  abrid  n  tiêêerci.  Acku  Rruman,  ma 
yeqsed  tamurt,  d  nger.  Di  tallit-nni,  nekk  ériɣ  ayen  yellan  di 
tezmert  n  Rruman,  acêal  n  yergazen  i  yellan,  ma  d  nitni  ur 
éran acêal n yergazen i zemreɣ ad d-sdukkleɣ i ṭṭrad. £ef waya, 
di yal timlilit yid-sen, ttefkeɣ-asen kan ayen iwulmen akken ad 
ten-qablen. Irgazen d yegran ugar. 
Ansa i d-ffɣen, ad d-afen lâeskeô Imaziɣen zdat-nsen, neɣ ad d-
êlellin  deffir-nsen,  teffɣen-d  am  zun  d  tiɣirdmiwin  si  ddaw 
tmurt.  Ansi  kkan  ad  afen  Imaziɣen  zwaren-ten  ɣer  wemkan. 
Nedda-asen  yiwet  yiwet,  armi  ççan  tiyita  di  yal  tama.  Di  yal 
timlilit, qbel ad akin ansi i asen-d-tekka tyita, Imaziɣen uffgen, 
ffɣen annar imenɣi. Nedda-asen am tasna n waôéen, tuqqsa ɣef 
tikkelt, affug ɣef tikkelt. 
Tewwev-d  tegrest,  iɣli-d  usemmiv,  ṭṭrad  yefra.  Lâeskeô  n 
Rruman  uɣen  amkan-nsen,  qqimen  anida  i  ten-tuɣ.  Di  tallit-
nni, akken yeéôa Albinus tettraê ôéaget, tetteddu ɣer uqerruy-
is, yuɣ abrid, yuɣal ɣer Ruma akken ad yessuter i Senat ad as-d-

yernu  lâesker.  Di  Tmazɣa,  yeooa-d  gma-s,  Aulus,  akken  ad 
yeêkem lâeskeô yellan. 
Di Ruma terwi gar-asen. yal tama tekkat akken ad teîîef Senat.  
Ur fran. Teqqim akken texôez. Tafrent23 ur d tezmir ad d tili.  
Di  Tmazɣa,  Aulus  yesla  amek  terwi  di  Ruma.  Yekker,  wissen 
yebɣa ad yezwir ad yekfu ṭṭṛad akken ad yawi iseɣ i yiri-s netta, 
neɣ yebɣa kan ad d-yesuffeɣ tuccar-is. Di yennayer n tegrest d 
usemmiv,  Aulus  yessuffeɣ-d  lâeskeô-is  akken  ad  nnaɣen  yid-
neɣ. Abrid-is amezwaru yedda ɣer teɣremt n Sutul24. 
Mi  nesla  s  tuffɣa-nni,  nuzzel  akken  ad  as-d-neg  afrag  i  Sutul. 
Qbel  ad  nawev,  nemlal  deg  webrid  widen  uzneɣ  akken  ad  d-
awin isalan si Sutul. Tiɣremt tefreg, agadir-is yezmer ad yeîîef 
tiyita.  Aulus  ur  yezmir  ad  yekcem.  Zzin-as  i  teɣremt    acêal  n 
wuvan  d  wussan,  wa  yekkat  wa  yekkat,  nekni  negguni-d  si 
tɣaltin, nenṭel. 
Aulus amcum, anekcum yebɣa ad yekcem tiɣremt, tugdi yugad 
ad  yaé  ɣer  zdat.  Yuki-yas  d  taqerêant.  Mi  neéra  tadyant-nni, 
nniɣ-asen  i wid yellan yid-i : ad nekker ad nqeôôeb ɣur-s, ad t-
-id-nesselqev netta d lâeskeô-is ɣer wennar ilaqen ; syin ad néer 
ma d imenɣi i ɣef iteddu Aulus, neɣ d askan n tezmert-is kan. 
Yella deg wawal n zik  di tmurt-nneɣ : "ma tseɣlev, wwet ! Ma 
ur tezmirev, ur sɣal ! D netta ara tt-id-yefrun. 
Ayen deg umi zwareɣ, fkiɣ widen ikecmen gar lâeskeô n Aulus. 
Yal tardast i ddan, yiwen seg-sen ad aɣ-d-yessiwev ayen yellan, 
anida llan, d wayen nnan.  Tga-yaɣ zun gar-asen i nella. 
Mi  aɣ-d-éran,  nekni  nteddu  zdat,  nitni  teddun  deffir-nneɣ, 
ooan  tiɣremt  n  Sutul  ɣer  deffir.  Tameddit  n  wass,  qbel  ad  d 
yeɣli  yiv,  Aulus  d  lâeskeô-is  gan  agraw  ad  nsen  deg  yiwen 
wegni.  Agni-nni  zzint-as-d  tewririn  si  yal  tama.  Amḍiq-nni 
nessen-it, nessen iberdan-is. Akken d yeɣli yiv, usan-d ɣur-neɣ 
wid-nneɣ  ssawven-aɣ  awal,  dɣa  nniɣ-asen  i  yifesyanen  yellan 
yid-i : 
- "Ad wen-d-iniɣ awal. Acêal n wussan aya i nessensar i Aulus. 
Nekni neéra ayen yellan, netta ur yeéri. Di ṭṭrad d axvaf. Win

yewten d amezwaru i yezwaren ɣer miêlal. Tamsalt n Aulus ad 
tt-nefru ass-a. A nekcem deg yiv tagrurt-is.  Yal yiwen seg-wen 
ad yekker ad iheggi lâeskeô-is". 
£as  éran  imenɣi  n  yiv  ur  yella  d  tanumi-nneɣ,  taggara  éran 
ilaq-aɣ ad tt-nefru. Mi asen-d-nniɣ awal-iw ssusmen, yal yiwen

yiwet,  awal  ur  yella.  Nekka-asen-d  si  tama  ufella,  nezzi-asen 
ɣef yidisan, ur yella wansa  ara rewlen. 
Mi  ériɣ  nezzi-d  akk  i  terbaât,  nga-asen  tameqyast,  neɣli  fell-
asen am akken tɣelli tmedda ɣef wewtul.  Qbel ad akin ad éran 
ayen yevran yid-sen, nekni nesserwet asgen deg gnen. Ur éran 
ad  rewlen  neɣ  ad  kkren  ad  wwten  ɣef  yiman-nsen.  Nadam, 
âeggu n tikli acêal n wussan akk d wesduqqes-nni,  abrid-nsen 
d anejli akka d wakka. Yekker herwel ameqqran deg wennar-
nni. Amur ameqqran seg-sen rewlen, dduklen ɣer yiwet tewrirt 
yellan  nnig  wemkan-nni.    Nurez  Aulus,  lâeskeô  neooa-ten  ad 
nesren,  amur  ameqqran  seg-sen  ur  yeddim  uzzal.  Yuɣ  lêal 
nezzi-d  akk  i  tmurt-nni.  Tevra  yid-sen  am  yiɣerdayen  deg

rewlen. Mi yuli wass, ssutreɣ-as i Aulus  ad ten-nefru. 
Si  tlemmast-nni  n  yiv,  si  mi  i  yasen-nekcem  annar,  nezzi-
yasen-d, nekk reffveɣ srusuɣ amek i d ixef-is temsalt-a.  Ayen 
bɣiɣ nekk, d abrid n tifrat nekni akk d Rruman. Imenɣi n wass-

nekni s Yimaziɣen, axsim ma yeɣli, yewwev tamurt, yexnunes, 
argaz  n  tissas  ur  as-irennu  tiyita.  S  webrid-nni  i  as-ddiɣ  i 
Aulus. Qqimeɣ ɣer tama-s, nniɣ-as : 
- Tusam-d ad aɣ-tennaɣem di tmurt-nneɣ. D kenwi i d-izegren 
ilel,  tkecmem-d  Tamazɣa-nneɣ.  Nekni  ur  nra  ṭṭṛad  nekni  d 
Öṛuman  ;  i  nessarem  kan  d  talwit,  yal  yiwen  ad  yeqqim  di 
tmurt-is,  ad  yeqqim  di  tlisa-s.  Taggara  tesseflem-d  acêal  n 
lâeskeô  ad  tgem  ṭṭṛad  deg  wakal-nneɣ.  Kečč  a  Aulus,  uɣal  ɣer 
tmurt-ik, siwev awal-iw i Senat di Ruma.  
Mi  as-kfiɣ  awalen-iw  i  Aulus,  ɣreɣ  i  sin  yergazen-nneɣ,  îîfen 
ixtucen,  ssutreɣ-asen  ad  bedden,  ad  gen  tawwurt  gar-asen,  si 
tama  ɣer  tayev.  Aulus  seg  tama-s,  yeɣra  i  lâesker-is  ad  sersen 
uzzal-nsen. Imenɣi yefra. 

- 27 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Seɣleɣ-as  i  Aulus  d  amezwaru,  yedda-d  s  leêder,  yekna,  yezri 
ddaw  yextucen-nni.  Syin,  wa  deffir  wa,  Iôumaniyen-nni,  zrin 
di tewwurt armi d aneggaru. 
Neooa-ten uɣalen d imedduren ɣer Utique. 
Mi yewwev wawal n twaɣit yevran ɣer Ruma, yekker deg-sen 
uferfud. Awal-nsen yiwen kan :"Amek d tella tifrat d Yugurten, 
amek  Aulus  yefka  awal  s  yisem  n  Ruma,  netta,  yugaden  ad 
yemmet,  yugad  ad  yewwet  s  yiɣil-is  yessers  ajenwi-is.  Awal  n 
Ruma  ala  Senat  i  yizemren  ad  t-yefk.  Aulus  nni  i  yaɣ-d- 
yewwin tacmat, awal-is ur deg-s azal !" 
Albinus, dadda-s n Aulus, yeéra tadyant n gma-s ɣer yixef-is i 
tezmer ad d-teddu, yesseêma awal akken Senat ad tt-yefru, ad 
d-yernu  lâeskeô  ɣer  Tmazɣa.  Di  tmerwi-nni,  Senat  yeggumma 
ad  yeddu  deg  wawal  n  Albinus,  yeggumma  ad  yernu  lâeskeô.  
Albinus yennuɣna, texreb-as twenza, syin yuɣ abrid n Tmazɣa, 
yekcem ɣer Utique. 
Nnan, mi d yusa kan si Ruma, ɣas di tlemmast n tegrest, yebɣa 
ad d-yesuffeɣ lâeskeô-is akken ad yerr ttaô n gma-s.  Mi yefhem 
tawaɣit deg llan lâeskeô-nni, yugad ad yeçç tiyita tis snat. Isers 
iman-is, yegguni tafsut, yegguni ass-is. 
Tadyant-nni  n  Aulus  terna-d  fellaɣ  aferfud.  Di  Ruma  cudden 
arkasen  akken  ad  d-rren  ttaô,  Albinus  ihegga  iman-is,  nekni 
neqqim,  newhem  amek  i  d  ixf-is.  Abrid-is  iban  sanda  i 
tetteddu. Ad yerɣ uzegzaw d uquran. Tilufa n Rruman nessen-
itent  acêal  aya.  Di  tazwara  kan  ssuffɣeɣ  aberraê  i  twizi 
tameqqrant. Yal tamurt ad tefk neɣ ad ternu irgazen. 
Ayen  i  aɣ-ixulfen  nekni  akk  d  Rruman  d  wa  :  nitni  sbedden 
tamurt-nsen ɣef tejmaât n Senat, adabu yella, lâeskeô yella. Yal

Di tikli-nni, Metellus yenwa iteddu anida i as-yehwa. Tidet-is, 
iteddu  anida  i  nra  nekni.  Tamurt    neɣ  tiɣremt  ur  nra  a  tt-
yekcem,  nteg-as-d  afrag  isennanen.  Acêal  n  tyita  i  yeçça  deg 
webrid-is.  Netta  iɣil  yeîîef  tamurt,  nekni  neéra  nesseksay-it 
akken ad yernu ad d yefk udem n tidet n Rruman. Akken daɣen 
at  tmurt-nneɣ  ad  éren  azal  n  tmeddurt  tilellit,  akken  ad  gen 
talast ger tudert n telwit, tudert tamaziɣt,  akk d tuqqna ddaw 
uzaglu n Rruman. 
Metellus,  giɣ-as  afrag  akken  ur  ikeççem  Sirta  akk  d  tiɣremtin 
nniven.  Ma deg wzaɣar, neooa-t yesserwet. Di tidet, tikli-ines 
tefka-d  i  at  tmurt-nneɣ  udem  n  Rruman.  Win  ur  t-nessin  zik, 
ass-a yessen-it, « win yenîeôôen ad yeqlileê !». 
Tudert n telwit tikwal tessufuɣ-d ayen n dir seg wayen yelhan.  
Ass-mi yella jedd-i Masensen d agellid, neɣ deffir-s di tgelda n 
Makawsen,    ulac  tiɣmert  n  tmurt  deg  ur  d  yella  yimenɣi  gar  
tiɣremtin,  ger  tuddar  neɣ  ger  txeôôubin.  Tikwal  d  imenɣi  ɣef 
wayen  deg  ur  yella  wazal  ;  ɣef  tlisa  n  tkessawt,  ɣer  terga  n 
waman  i  tissit  n  tebêirin,  neɣ  tikwal  ɣef  snat  turdas  n  wakal.  
Yal  tikkelt  tettawev  ɣer  tummeét,  ɣer  ucangal,  timseggeft  neɣ 
aneccab. Mi ɣlint tmegrav, syin ad uɣalen i tuzzma, i "tenniv-
iyi-d, nniɣ-as". Di tallit-nni, ur éran ur ssinen acengu n beôôa. 
Imir,  acengu-nsen  d  atmaten-nsen,  d  loaô-nsen,  neɣ  d  win 
icerwen tidi yid-sen. Tilisa n tmurt, ur tent-éeôôen, ur llant deg 
wallaɣ-nsen.    Tilisa  n  tmurt  beâdent  fell-asen  akken  yebâed 
igenni ɣef tmurt. 
Tikli n Metellus, nekk ɣur-i, tusa-d akken  ad tekkes tidderɣelt- 
a n at tmurt-nneɣ. Ansi i yezri Metellus ad yeoo imeîîawen, ad 
yeoo  taɣennant  n  at  tmurt  i  yisem  n  Rruman.  £as  ulac  ticrav 
nebla  idammen,    tallit-nni  ur  nra  ad  tiɣzif.    Yal  tikkelt  neéra

neooa-ten  d  imedduren.  Mi  sen-nenna  awalen  iseggmen,  
amur seg-sen uɣalen d lâeskeɣ-nneɣ, ddan yid-neɣ.

Massinissa et Hannibal. Hannibal pare un javelot avec son bouclier et abat le cheval 
de  son  adversaire.  Massinissa  se  relève  et, a  pied,  s'élance  vers  Hannibal,  à  travers 
une grêle de traits, qu'il reçoit sur son bouclier en peau d'éléphant. Il arrache un des 
javelots et vise Hannibal qu'il manque encore. Pendant qu'il en arrache un autre, il 
est blessé au bras et se retire un peu à l'écart... Sa blessure bandée, il revient dans la 
mêlée,  sur  un  autre  cheval.  La  lutte  reprend  avec  un  nouvel  acharnement,  car  les 
soldats sont excités par la présence de leurs chefs. Hannibal voit ses soldats fléchir 
peu  à  peu,  certains  s'éloignent  du  champ  de  bataille  pour  panser  leurs  blessures, 
d'autres se retirent définitivement. Il se porte partout, encourage ses hommes, abat 
par-ci,  par-là  ses  adversaires,  mais  ses  efforts  demeurent  vains.  Désespéré,  il  ne 
pense qu'à sauver les restes de son armée. Il s'élance en avant, entouré de quelques 
cavaliers, se fraie un chemin et quitte le champ de bataille. Massinissa qui l'aperçoit 
se lance avec son groupe derrière lui. Il le presse, malgré la douleur que lui cause sa 
blessure, car il brûle de le ramener prisonnier. Hannibal s'échappe à la faveur de la

Abrid yergel, ad nuɣal ɣer Sirta !

ad tili tifrat gar-aneɣ, nekk akk d Metellus.

wass usan-d isalan si Ruma : « Senat yefka tamurt n Numidya i

zik,  ass-en  yekkes  ukukru.    Senat  n  Rruman  di  Ruma  yefka

Ayen i umi xemmeɣ tazwara, maççi i yat tmurt-iw yeddren am

timlilit-nni ihegga, d ticeôket, d tasraft deg  ara yessedrem wid 
yumnen awal-is. 
Iberdan n tifrat reglen-d, i aɣ-d-yeggran ala abrid n yiseɣ. 
Nekker fell-aɣ, nezzi i tmurt, nga aberraê akken ad d-nesbedd 
irgazen  ara  yekksen  aɣilif  n  Rruman.    Yal  tamurt  seg  nekka 
nufa  nnig  n  wayen  i  nesarem.  Yal  tamurt  seg  yezri  Metellus, 
anda  i  yesserɣ  igran  d  tizeɣwa,    nufa  atmaten-nneɣ    kkren-d 
akken llan.  Avu n tnekra isuv-d i tôuzi uzaglu n Rruman , yuɣ  
yal tamurt. 
Mi d-nessemlal irgazen-nneɣ, nuɣ iberdan seg yekka Metellus. 
Yal tamurt seg yezri nerra-yasen-d asirem.  Imukan anda llan 
Rruman  nessenger-iten,  anda  ur  llan  nerna-d  irgazen.  Akken 
armi nesmed ajemmal ameqqran. 
Deg wedwi-nni, llan  iɣerman i aɣ-yezwaren i tnekra, kkren i 
tyita  n  Rruman.  Tiɣremt  n  Begga  tezwar-itent.    Tadyant-nni 
teôṛeẓ asalu i tnekra mgal Rruman. 
Deg wass amenzu n tefsut, tiɣremt teççur d lâeskeô n Rruman. 
At  Begga  cudden-tt.  I  yimensi  n  tefsut,  yal  Amaziɣ  n  Begga 
yessekcem-d  inebgi  yiwen  neɣ  sin  seg  lâeskeô-nni.  Taggara 
gan-asen timecreḍt, teçça-ten tefrut, ur d-yeggri yiwen seg-sen.  

- 40 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Wid  yellan  di  beôôa,  ur  yella  anda  ara  rewlen.  Tiwwura  n 
teɣremt  medlent,    ixammen  deg  zedɣen  gan-asen-d  afrag 
Imaziɣen. Zzin-asen imezdaɣ, wa s uneccab wa s ujenwi,  armi 
ten-snegren. I d-yeggran seg-sen d ameddur ala afesyan-nsen, 
T. Turpilius.  Ooan-t  at Begga d ameddur, yuɣal ɣer Utique. 
Dinna di Utique, Iôumaniyen êekmen-as s lmut, nɣan-t. 
Si tedyant-nni n Begga i aɣ-yekkes unezgum. Nekk, kkseɣ ccek 
deg yiman-iw : aéar n tnekra yella deg yidammen-nneɣ ; yella 
ugerru  neɣ  ur  yella,  yal  amdan  n  tmurt-nneɣ  yezdeɣ  deg-s 
uéar-nni  n  yiseɣ  i  seg  ur  iqebbel  tabarda  n  yemnekcem.  At 
Begga kkren, begsen, cuddden-tt  gar-asen,  taggara ksen  isem 
n Rruman di teɣremt-nsen. Ass-a éran, ayen yebɣu yili ɣer zdat, 
nitni  huccen,  sengugin  adabu  n  Rruman  s    yiɣallen  n  tdukli-
nsen. £as, taggara, ur sen-tdum tallit-nni. 
Tadyant  n  Begga  akken  i  tt-neéra  nekni  d  iseɣ  ameqqran  mi 
yewwev  wawal  n  twaɣit-is  ɣer  Rruman,  ɣer  Metellus  akk  d 
Marius.  Mi  yessawev  Turpilius  ɣer  Utique,  ala  netta  i  d 
ameddur,    tuɣal-asen    am  wid  yedrewcen.  Ur  fhimen  amek 
imezdaɣ  n  Begga  réan  lqanun  n  Rruman,  nɣan  lâeskeô  n 
Rruman !  Tuɣal-asen-d teêsift, d taɣennant n war talast. 
Qbel  ad  slen lâeskeô n  Rruman  s  tedyant  yevran,  qbel  ad  ten-
yekcem uferfud, qbel ad beddlen tikli-nsen, anda ad teddun ad 
éeôôen  lexyal  n  watmaten-nsen  yemmuten  di  Begga,  Metellus 
icudd  arkasen-is.  Ur  d-zzin  sin  neɣ  tlata  wussan  mi  d-yessuli  
ajemmal n lâeskeô, abrid-is ɣer Begga akken ad yerr ttaô. 
Iseɣ deg-neɣ i yella, lâaô deg-neɣ i yella. 
Yal  tamurt  akka.  Yal  tamurt  i  tekcem  tmurt  nniven,    amur 
ameqqran  s  ufus  n  at  tmurt-nni.  Anida  ur  yella  ufus,  ur  yella 
yemnekcem. Akka tadyant n Begga. 
Mi  teddun  lâeskeô  n  Metellus  ɣer  teɣremt  n  Begga,  qbel  ad 
awven  tiwwura  n  teɣremt,  yesbedd-iten  Metellus  deg  webrid. 
Yezwer  ɣer  zdat  imnayen  Imaziɣen  yellan  yid-s.  Iga-ten 
Metellus d afrag ɣer zdat.  Mi wwven timizar n Begga, asurif 
kan  qbel  tawwurt,    akken  ten-id-éran  imezdaɣ-is,  ur  gan 
anezgum. Nwan d imnayen-nneɣ. Udem-nsen d Imaziɣen, iles-
nsen  d  tamaziɣt.  Si  tmuɣli-nni,  iâessasen  n  teɣremt  akk  d 
ifellaêen  yellan  deg  tebêirin-nsen  qqimen  di  tfellaêt-nsen, 
tiwwura n teɣremt ooan-tent llint. Si mi kecmen yemnayen-nni

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

n  Metellus  ɣer  Begga,  taggara  zzin-d  ɣer  deffir,  srewten  wid 
yellan  zdat-sen,  nɣan  wid  i  ten-id-iqublen,  urzen  tiwwura  n 
teɣremt, syin yeflali-d Metellus s lâeskeô-is Iôumaniyen, yekcem 
Begga. Yekker usuɣu di teɣremt, Rruman yekcem tasga. Lâeskeô 
n Metellus nɣan wid nɣan, sserɣen tizeɣwa n teɣremt, hudden 
ayen hudden. Cudden imeêbas fernen, wid ara yawin d aklan-
nsen. 
Si  tyita-nni  n  Begga,  nekk  kkseɣ  layas  n  tefrat  si  tama  n 
Rruman. Ayen i umi zemren xedmen-t.  Tikli n Metellus akk d 
Marius  tban am uzal. I yaɣ-d-yegran yid-sen d ajenwi ! 
èriɣ amennuɣ mgal Rruman ad yiɣzif. Ilmend n wedham kan n 
lâeskeô  n  Rruman  deg  yimenɣiyen  imeqqranen,  alamma  tama 
tekka  di  tayev,  nekk  ddiɣ  abrid  nniven.  Ilaq-aɣ  ad  nesseɣzef 
imenɣi, a ten nesefcel yiwet yiwet alamma imeqqranen n Ruma 
ttun tadyant n Tmazɣa.  Ad nesseɣzef imenɣi, ad newwet akken 
ur  d  rennun  lâeskeô  si  Ruma,  syin  ad  d-yas  wass  ad  ibeddel 
wudem  n  Senat  di  Ruma.  Nessarem  ad  d  nemlil  ɣer  zdat 
imɣaren  wid  ukud  ara  nemsefham,  wid  ukud  ara  d-nefsi 
tundar. 
Sin  yiderma-nni  n  Senat,  popular akk d  nobilis, d amjadel yal 
ass  anwa  ara  yaɣen  adabu  n  Senat.  Yal  tama  tekkat  s  wayes 
tezmer,  s  tidet  neɣ  s  tfukal,  akken  ad  d-teîîef  tasawent.  Seg 
wass  ɣer  wayev,  tezmer  ad  tbeddel  udem.  Wid  d-yefkan 
Metellus  ɣer  Tmazɣa,  yezmer  ad  yeṛôeé  wawal-nsen  ;  azekka 
ad  asen  deffir-nsen  wid  ara  as-d-yeɣren  i  Metellus  ad  yuɣal 
akin netta d lâeskeô-is. 
£as abrid imenɣi yenjeô, abrid n tifrat ur t-nettu. 
I  Metellus  fkiɣ-as  wid  ad  t-yessedhun,  i  Ruma  uzneɣ  i  wid 
yellan dinna ad ṣṣiwven awal-iw i wid yesseddun Senat akk d 
wid  ssarmeɣ  ad  kecmen    tazeqqa n Curia ɣer Senat si sya ɣer 
zdat. 
Zziɣ i tmurt akken tella. Yal azaɣar, yal adrar kkiɣ-as-d akken 
ad  nessemɣer  tanekra.  Yal  tamurt  nekcem,  amager  yiwen-is  : 
tawaɣit n Rruman tewwev-iten neɣ slan yes-s, irgazen heggan i  
twizi.  Wid i d-yuɣalen seg yimenɣiyen êkan-asen tidyanin deg 
llan. 
Mi d tusa tegrest, amur ameqqran n lâeskeô n Metellus uɣalen 
ɣer  tmurt  n  Carthage,  wid  yeqqimen  deg  wakal  n  Tmazɣa

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

sdurin  iman-nsen  deffir  ifergan  n  tregwa  i  ɣzen  deg  wakal, 
tisulal  n  wesɣar  d  wuzzal.  Qqimen,  ggunin  ussan  n  tefsut.  
Nekni ncudd-itt, nuzzel akessar d usawen  i tnekra. 
Tallit-nni, seg wakken rriɣ tamuɣli-w i yimenɣi mgal Rruman, 
anda rezfeɣ ufiɣ at tmurt-iw, meééi neɣ meqqer,  begsen i twizi 
tameqqrant, nwiɣ nezmer i wedrar ad t-nerr d luva. Udem-nni 
n  tdukli  yessefreê-iyi.  Uɣaleɣ  ttuɣ  tilufa-nni  akk  yellan  gar  at 
tmurt.  S  tmuɣli-nni  n  tdukli  gar-aneɣ deg lliɣ, tadukli-nni am 
ivudan ufus,  i d-yeɣli fell-i wesyax n Bumelxiô. 
Bumelxiô yella am gma neɣ ugar. Anda ur lliɣ, d netta i d awal-
iw, d netta i d tiîî-iw. Neddukel, nemyussan si zik n zik.  Nedda 
lwaêid  di  teméi,  deg  yimenɣi,  di  talwit.  D  netta  dɣa  i  ɣef 
ttekleɣ,  fkiɣ-t  ad  yesselqem  awal  nekni  d  Metellus.    Bumelxiô 
yessen Rruman, yessen amek tetteddu tmurt-nsen. 
Nekk ɣileɣ ad yessedhu Metellus, ad t-yesgen s wawal akken ad 
nezzuɣer  imenɣi  ar  d-yas  wass  n  tifrat,  Bumelxiô  yuɣ  abrid 
nniven. 
Di  tazwara  ur  umineɣ.  Bumelxir  yellan  am  gma,  ur  nwiɣ  ad 
yas seg-s uɣurru. 
Acêal  n  tikkal  mi  ara  neqqim,  netta  ad  yuɣal  ɣer  wawal-nni-
ines : "ilaq-aɣ ad nefru nekni d Rruman ; ur nezmir i yimenɣi 
mgal adrar n Rruman ... uɣal ɣer Ruma, suter leânaya n Senat, 
ad sen-nefk ayen yellan d lfil, d agmer neɣ d agerruɣ n wureɣ ; 
taggara, awi-d kan ad aɣ-ooen ...". 
Yal tikkelt ad ten-id-yesni wawalen-agi, nekk ad as-iniɣ, ad as-
alseɣ  i  Bumelxiô  abrid  i  éôiɣ  :  "  Rruman  ur  ssinen  talast  nnig 
talast n yiɣil-nsen. Wid yellan zik, wid yefran d Masensen, wid 
iqudren  awal-nsen  nitni  d  Makawsen,  ass-a  negren.  Wid  d 
yegran  di  Ruma,  d  wid  i  yenwan  timura  akk  nsen.  Anida 
tewwev  tiî-nsen  ad  ɣillen  d  ayla-nsen  nitni.  Nekk  ssneɣ-ten, 
ériɣ  amek  éerren  timura  ass-mi  lliɣ  yid-sen  deg  yimenɣi  n 
Numance di Spanya. Tawant tesuffuɣ  ɣer yir iberdan. Akken i 
yasen-tevra i Yiôumaniyen. £illen ddunit tebna ɣef  yiɣil neɣ ɣef 
yixef ujenwi, maççi ɣef tmussni akk d leqder n tlisa. Akka i llan 
nitni." 
Akken  i  as-kkiɣ  i  Bumelxiô,  netta  ad  d  yezzi  ɣer  wawal-nni  n 
kennu. Yeqqim-as zun d tanicca yentan deg wallaɣ-is.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Acengu  yellan  ɣer  zdat,  ayen  d  yusan  seg-s  tebniv  fell-as. 
Tiêila, tiḥḥeṛci, yal tifexxet tezmer ad d tili, yal tiyita tezmer ad 
ternu. Acengu n zdat, zwir-it ɣer tyita qbel ad k-yezwir, zwir-it 
ɣer  tsawent  qbel  ad  k-yezwir.  Ma  d  acengu  ara  d-yeffɣen 
deffir-k,  acengu  ara  d-ilalen  gar  watmaten-ik,  winna  ur  tella 
deg-s  tewwurt.    Tiyita  n  deffir  ur  tebniv  fell-as,    tqeôôeê, 
tesefcal ugar, tettôué ifadden. 
Akka tiyita n Bumelxiô, tekka-yi-d si deffir ur bniɣ fell-as. 
Ger webrid n yiseɣ i deg ara nekkes azaglu ɣef Tmazɣa, netta 
yefren abrid n kennu zdat Rruman, syin yuɣ abrid n tixxubta. 
Nekk  nniɣ-as  ad  yesgen  Metellus,  taggara  yuɣal-iyi  d  afus  n 
Metellus i tyita deg watmaten-is. 
Cudden-tt,  xerzen-tt.  Metellus,  Bumelxiô  akk  d  wid  nniven, 
gan tifexxet akken ad aɣ-arzen, ad aɣ-cudden d imedduren. S 
ufus  n  Bumelxiô,  Metellus  yegguni  ad  aɣ-awin  ɣur-s  ncudd 
avar afus.  Taggara, tirga-nni ur as-teffiɣ i Metellus. 
Yiwen  wass,  yewwev-iyi-d  wawal  s  tesraft-nni  i  gan  qbel  ad 
neɣli  deg-s.  Tabrat-nni  d  yusan  ger  ifassen  n  Nabdales    syin 
tewwev-d  ger  ifassen-iw  tefra-tent-id.  Ur  yella  din  ccek. 
Tadyant teqqen, tefra, nekk ur ukiɣ. 
Ass-mi d nurez Bumelxiô, nesuter-as ad aɣ-d-yessefôez iberdan 
i  t-yeṣṣawven  ɣer  taluft-agi.  Awal-is  yegzem  :  "d  keçč  a 
Yugurten  i  d  afrag  i  tifrat  nekni  d  Rruman.  Ma  tettwakksev 
keçč, ad tili tifrat gar-aneɣ. Nra tamurt-nneɣ, nra talwit, ma d 
keçč  teggumav  ad  tefkev  udem.  Ansi  i  ak-d-nekka,  ur  d  nufa 
tawwurt...". 
Awalen-nni  n  Bumelxiô,  win  akken  ukkud  nuzzel,  nennuɣ 
Aôumani  acêal  d  aseggas,  ass-a  yuɣ  abrid  n  kennu  zdat 
yemnekcem.  Awalen-nni  n  Bumelxiô,  mi  sen-selleɣ,  nekk  lliɣ 
selleɣ i tiêeôci n Metellus. 
Metellus  yessekcem-d  tawekka  gar-aneɣ  ur  ukiɣ.  Akken 
fehmeɣ  tamsalt,  banet-d  têila  i  as-yenna  Metellus  i  Bumelxiô 
akken ad t-yeṣṣiwev ɣer talast agi. Yenna-yas Metellus ; "keçč a 
Bumelxir,  Senat  n    Ruma  ur    yezmir  ad  ak-yessuref  seg-mi 
tegrev  afus  di  lmut  n  Masiwen  di  tlemmast  n  Ruma.  Azekka 
nezmer ad nefru  nekni d Yugurten. Nezmer ad d-naf tawwurt 
i  ṭṭrad-agi  yellan  gar-aneɣ.  Tella  yiwet,  ma  nefra  d  Yugurten, 
tifrat-nni  ara  d-yilin  ad  teglu  s  uqerruy-ik  keçč.  Senat  ad  d-

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

yessuter  ad  k-nawi  tcuddev  ɣer  Ruma  akken  ad  k-ncaôeâ 
dinna, Yugurten yeqbel ad yefk afus deg-k." 
Awal-nni  asekkak  n  Metellus,  yenta-as  deg  wul  i  Bumelxiô, 
yumen  tikerkas  n  Metellus.  Ikellex-it  yir  akellex,  am  zun  d 
aqcic  ameéyan.  Teçça-as  i  Metellus.  Taggara,  Bumelxiô  yuɣal 
am zun d asafu, ireq yettaé ɣer zdat. 
Mi nefra côeâ n Bumelxiô, ur d yegra liser, ur d tegra tiéeḍt n 
tmeddurt.  £as  Bumelxiô  yemmut,  lexyal-is  yezdeɣ-aɣ.  Wid 
yefkan afus yid-s, wa yemmut am netta, wa yerwel ɣer tmurt n 
Carthage, yedda d Rruman. 
Tawekka  tekcem-d  tasga.  Ma  yella  Bumelxiô  ass-a  yefka  afus, 
yal  yiwen  seg  wiyav  yezmer  azekka  ad  yefk  afus,  d  Nabdales 
neɣ d wayev. Refdeɣ serseɣ, ufiɣ d adway kan i d ixef-is.  Nnan 
zik  « ma teddiv d wasif ur yezmir ad k-yawi wasif ». Tamurt i 
ɣer  wwveɣ,    qbel  ad  serseɣ,  ad  seroeɣ  i  tikli  anda  nniven.  
Amkan anda lliɣ d wemkan s anda tedduɣ uɣallen ttin, xerzen 
am  tundar  uxeôôaz.  Anda  qqimeɣ  i  wuççi,  tiêdert  n  weɣrum 
aquran, taɣenjawt neɣ snat n seksu, nek kkreɣ. Awal n tisin n 
Yugurten akk d wawal n tuɣalin n Yugurten, mlalen. Ur yeéra 
yiwen anwa ass i d-usiɣ neɣ anwa ass i zriɣ, beddleɣ tamurt. S 
tikli-nni n yal ass, safesseɣ amur uɣilif i d-yeɣlin fell-i. 
Tiyita n Metellus, ilaq ad as-tuɣal. Anda yella Rruman fkiɣ-asen 
wid  ara  ten-yesduqqsen.  Akken  daɣ  wid-nneɣ  ad  asen-yekkes 
wefcal-nni,  ilaq-asen  ad  rren  udem-nsen  i  yimenɣi  mgal 
Uôumani.  Yal  tamurt  tekker,  tezzi-yasen  i  lâesker  n  Rruman  i 
yellan dinna. 
Nekk abrid-iw friɣ-t. 
Tedduɣ uvan ussan akken ad afeɣ anida yella Metellus. £as di 
tazwara  ttweṣṣiɣ  akken  ur  t-tekkat  tyita,  akken  ur  t-yettawev 
uneccab,  ad  d-yeqqim  yedder,  d  axûim,  azekka  ad  nemsefma 
yid-s,  ass-a tallit tbeddel. Netta yewwev-d s aqerruy-iw, nekk 
ad  qesdeɣ  aqerruy-is.    Tedduɣ,  simmal  sseqrabeɣ  ɣer  lateô-is. 
Tuɣal  gar-aneɣ  am  wemcic  d  uɣerda.  Tedduɣ  ad  t-id-îîfeɣ  am 
uɣerda deg umeôdax. Yal yiwen yekkat ad yezwir wayev. Netta 
yeéra, nekk ériɣ.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Di  teɣremt  n  Tala28,  qrib  i  nemlal.  Rziɣ  ɣer  din  akken  ad  d 
kkseɣ  syin  arraw-iw.  £as  amkan  yefreg,  ufiɣ  yeqreb  tamurt  n 
Carthage. Metellus yezmer ad  yedwi ɣer din. Ur zrin sin neɣ  
kôad wussan  seg-mi d-ffɣeɣ tiɣremt-nni mi yewwev Metellus s 
lâeskeô-is. 
Zzin-as  i  Tala,  ssulin  tisulal  i  yeâricen  akken  ad  kken  nig 
wefrag, nnig icerfan yezzin i teɣremt. Gan ayen i umi zemren 
akken  ad  kecmen  Tala.    Metellus  yenwa  din  i  lliɣ.  Isdukel-d 
ayen yellan d lâesker ɣer din, iɣil ad yekfu din ṭṭṛad n Tmazɣa s 
tuîîfa  n  Yugurten.  Nnig  waggur  imenɣi  d  wamek  kecmen 
Iôumaniyen Tala. 
Ass-mi wwveɣ ɣer  din, deffir tiyita-nni n Metellus,    d  nnger i 
yevran di teɣremt. Riɣ ad éreɣ s wallen-iw. Ur d yegra ugadir 
ibedden,  ur  d  yegra  useklu  ibedden,  ur  d  tegra  tmazirt 
yezgezwen.    Anda  yewwev  ufus  n  Rruman,  yeooa-d  ixeôban, 
tabuxt d lmut ɣer deffir. Inagan i d-yegran d imedduren, d wid 
kan  ineṭlen  di  tmizar  n  Tala.  D  tisselbi  kan  i  asen-d-yegran. 
Gran-d, ur mmuten, ur ddiren. 
Tadyant n Tala yeffeɣ wawal-is di Tmazɣa. Imdanen éran ayen 
i  umi  yezmer  Rruman,  anda  yezmer  ad  yessiwev.  Acengu  ara 
yesiɣen times i teɣremt akken s yimezdaɣ-is, ur yelli usirem ad 
yas liser seg-s. Imenɣi yekker, ad tekk tama di tayev. Yal yiwen 
yeéra iman-is. 
Tikwal  llan  isalan  yessefraêen,  llan  wid  yesseqraêen.  Di 
teɣremt  n  Lebda29,  imdanen  uɣen  abrid  nniven.  Anda  ilaq  ad 
fergen  tiɣremt-nsen,  nitni  uɣen  tama  n  Rruman.  Ssutren  i 
Metellus  ad  asen-d-yernu  lâesker  akken  ad  yili  d  afrag  fell-
asen. 
At  Lebda  ur  llan  d  Imaziɣen  deg  iéuran-nsen.  Amur  ameqran 
seg-sen  usan  d  si  tmurt  n  Tyr.  £as  iles-nsen  yuɣal  d  Amaziɣ, 
nitni ooan laâwayed n tmurt seg d usan. Ṭṭṛad n Tmazɣa, zun 
nitni  ur  ten  id  yewwiv.  Anda  ilaq  ad  begsen  ɣef  yiman-nsen, 
nitni  malen  ɣer  win  ugaden.  Ssutren  leânaya  i  Metellus  d 
lâesker-is.  Kksen-d  iman-nsen  seg  wakal-nni  ɣef  teddun,  rran 

                                                            
28 Di teɣremt n Tala i d kkren, i llan zedɣen warraw n Yugurten. 
29 Lebda = Leptis Magna (di tmurt n Libya)

iman-nsen  ddaw  leânaya  n  win  d  yusan  s  ibabuôen  si  tmurt 
yellan akin, agemmav i yilel. 
Tamurt tekker, tiwizi mgal Rruman tbeddel udem-is. Akken ad 
d-nernu  irgazen,  zegreɣ  tiniri  ɣer  watmaten-nneɣ  Imucaɣ  i 
yellan din. £as ur aɣ-qriben, tecrek-aɣ tmurt. Rruman ma yeîîef 
Tamazɣa  ufella,  tama  deg  anda  nella  nekni,  azekka  ad  yawev  
tamurt n wadda. Acengu ilaq ad as-tgev talast  akin, ansi kan i 
d-yekcem.  D  awalen-a  i  asen-nniɣ  i  yat  tmurt  n  wadda. 
Taggara, rran-d awal, nnig wayen ssarmeɣ. Aéar-nni n tnekra 
akken  yella  ɣur-neɣ  i  yella  ɣur-sen.    Ass-mi  d  uɣaleɣ  syin,  d 
timrawin n yemnayen i d-yeddan yid-i. 
Tamurt  n  wadda  kkseɣ-tt  deg  weɣbel,  tekker,  syin  qesdeɣ 
tamurt ugellid Buxus, Tamazɣa utaram. 
Ilaq-aɣ ad nessemɣer admer n imenɣi mgal Rruman. Ilaq-aɣ ad 
nesdukel  iɣallen-nneɣ  akken  ad  nessemɣer  tiyita.  Di  tazwara, 
Buxuc ur tewwiv temsalt. Ur yella d aêbib, ur yella d acengu n 
Rruman.    Maca,  tella  yiwet.  Ma  Rruman  yuɣ  tamurt  nneɣ, 
abrid-is  iban,  tikli-s  tban,  azekka  ad  yewwet  ad  yessihrew. 
Azekka  ad  yawev  tilisa  n  Buxuc.  Maççi  d  asif  n  talast,  asif  n 
Melwen30, ara t-id-yerren ɣer deffir. 
D  awalen  agi  i  as-nniɣ  i  Buxuc.  £as  nemyussan,  nemcarak, 
yelli-s deg wexxam-iw i tella, sawleɣ-as am akken ara yessiwel 
wemdan 
tmurt,  yesdukel-aɣ  uéar, 
tesdukel-aɣ tmeslayt, sduklen-aɣ idammen. Acengu d yusan ɣer 
yiwen,  yusa-d  ɣer  wayev.  Ur  tella trewla, ur tella tdarit deffir 
wuffal,  yecban  awal-nni  "axxam  n  baba  yerɣa,  meqqar  ad 
sseêmuɣ".  Times n Rruman ur tferreq ger tzeqqa ma tella akka 
neɣ akin i talast. 
Buxuc yuɣ abrid n yiseɣ, ibges-d i tnekra mgal Metellus. 
Mi  nefra  nekk  akk  d  Buxuc,  nesemlal-d  lâeskeô-nneɣ  deg 
uzaɣar  akken  ad  sen-nesefhem  tamsalt  i  yifesyanen  n  Buxuc. 
Din i yasen-nniɣ ass-nni : 
" -Yal tamurt tefka leqder i tlisa-s, yal tamurt tbedd i tudert di 
tmurt ur tettili ddaw uzaglu n win ara d-yasen ansi nniven. Si 

tesdukel-aɣ 

i  gma-s. 

                                                            
30  Asif  n  Melwen  (Muluca  =  Malva  =  Moulouya)  :  talast  ger  tmurt  n  Numidya, 
tagelda  ugellid  Yugurten  akk  d  Tmazɣa  utaram  (Maurétanie),  tagelda  n  ugellid 
Buxuc (Bocchus).

zik  n  zik,  tudert-nneɣ  tebna  ɣef  tlelli.  Nekni  d  Imaziɣen  ur 
nessin  azaglu  d  tirni.  Ass-a  ur  nezgir  asif,  ur  nezgir  ilel  a 
nekcem  tamurt  n  medden.  Rruman  d-ikecmen  tamurt-nneɣ  
yezger-d ilel yusa-d ad yerr tamurt-nneɣ ddaw uzaglu. Ur yella 
d  ayen  ara  neqbel.  Anwa  deg-wen  ara  iqeblen  azaglu  n 
Rruman ? 
Imdanen,  tiɣremtin,  timura,  di  ddiq  i  d  tettban  tdukli-nsen. 
Ass-a,  aqlaɣ  neddukel  acku  tesdukel  aɣ  temsalt,  sduklen  aɣ 
iéuran,  yesdukel-aɣ  uzekka.  Yezmer  uzekka  ad  yili  d  tafat  ma

wass-a  tefka-aɣ-d  tafat  ara  aɣ-yessiwven  akin  i  yiɣil,  akin  ɣer 
wussan anda imdanen ur kennun ddaw uzaglu. Tamurt tekker, 
d kenwi i d iɣil-is, d afud-is, d azekka usirem-ines." 
Nebda tikli, abrid-nneɣ ɣer Sirta. 
Si  tedyant  n  Begga,  n  Tala  akk  d  tiɣremtin  nniven,  Metellus 
yekcem s lâesker tiɣremtin nniven. Di taggara ur riɣ ad yernu 
ad yesserɣ yal tiɣremt n Tmazɣa. Si tedyant-nni n Begga akk d 
Tala,  yal  tiɣremt  seg  ara  zriɣ,  ttiniɣ-asen  yiwen  wawal  :  ma 
yusa d Rruman, ooet tiwwura n tiɣremt llint. £as yekcem ass-a, 
azekka  ad  yeffeɣ,  ad  yafeg  am  tagut  unebdu.  Yif  ad  yekcem 
tiɣremt  ibedden  wala  ad  yesserɣ  ayen  nebna  deg  wacêal 
iseggassen. 
Akken  i  teffeɣ.  Anida  yewwev  Metellus  akk  Marius,  ad  afen 
tiɣremt  llint  tewwura-s.  Netta  iɣil  malen  ɣur-sen  imezdaɣ, 
nekni neooa beddent tiɣremtin-nneɣ, ddren watmaten-nneɣ. 
Tadukli  n  lâesker-nneɣ  akk  d  wid  n  Buxuc,  abrid-is  yiwen. 
Nefra  ɣef  Metellus  ad  as-nekkes  aqerru.  Ur  yella  webrid 
nniven. 
Anida  yella  ad  neɣli  fell-as.  Ma  yeffeɣ  si  Tmazɣa,  ad  t-nevfer 
alamma  d  Utique,  di  tmurt  n  Carthage,  ula  d  tin  d  tamurt-
nneɣ. Nefra, ad d-nuɣal s uqerru-s, anida yebɣa yeffer. 
Deg  webrid  n  Sirta,  nebda  nettheggi  imenɣi  mgal  lâesker  n 
Rruman. Imenɣi yezmer ad yili zdat n Sirta, di Tiddis, neɣ deg 
uzaɣar.  D  Metellus  ad  d-yefken  tasarut-is.  Sirta  nefra  ad  tt-
nekcem, ad nerr tiɣremt i yimawlan-is. Syin tamsalt n Metellus 
ad tefru din neɣ anda nniven. 
Mi  yesla  Metellus  s  tdukli-nneɣ,  iga  anezgum  ameqqran. 
Tiêeôci-nni n Rruman s wayla-s. Metellus yewwet ad aɣ-yebvu

nekk  akk  d  Buxuc.  Tifukal  yessedda  i  Bumelxiô,  yewwet  ad

Tadyant  teqqim  akken,  ger  yemnayen d yuzen Metellus  akk d

Tusa-d tegrest, yal yiwen yuɣal ɣer wemkan-is, ṭṭṛad ad yekker 
mi ara kksen igefran imeqqranen, ar d-fsin ideflawen.  
 
 
Tallit n Marius Caius akk d Sulla 
 

Yiwen wass yusa-aɣ-d wawal amaynut ; yusa-d si Senat 
n Ruma : Marius yettwafren, yuɣal d netta i d consul (jiniral) 
di  Ruma.  Fran  ad  yas  ɣer  Numidya  deg  wemkan  n  Metellus. 
Imir  Marius  yuɣal  ɣer  Ruma,  yella  din  di  tefrent-nni,  yezger 
nnig lebɣi n Metellus. 
S  isalan  i  d-yusan  si  Ruma  nefhem  s  uzuɣer-nni  i  yezzuɣur 
irennu  Metellus.  Si  tazwara-as,  ziɣ  d  asedhu  kan  i  yaɣ 
yessedhuy. Tamsalt teffeɣ-as afus. 
Nefhem tamuɣli n Ruma : Iôumaniyen ur beddlen tamuɣli-nsen 
ɣef  tmurt-nneɣ.  Anda  ara  d-llin  tiwwura  i  telwit,  ad  d-aznen 
ɣur-i  akken  ad  d  naf  abrid  n  tifrat,  nitni  fernen  Marius,  win 
ara yesseêmun ṭṭṛad ugar, win ara yernun tardast n tmes akin 
ɣef tlufa n Metellus.  
Marius  ssneɣ-t  di  ṭṭṛad  n  Numance,  d  aâessekriw  deg 
yidammen  nnig  akk  ifesyanen  n  Rruman.  D  argaz  n  wawal, 
iêemmel  tamurt-is.  Mi  yella  ddaw  Metellus,  ur  as-fsin  i

yiɣallen, icudd-it Metellus. Ass-a d netta uɣur d tegra. Fehmeɣ, 
ad as-nuɣal i temsalt seg wadda. 
Di tefsut d yusan  i nesla yezger-d Marius  ɣer Utique, yerna-d 
ibabuôen  n  lâeskeô.  Ass-mi  d  yusa  Marius,  Metellus  tuɣ-it 
yezger  akin,  yuɣal  ɣer  tmurt-is.  Ur  ira  ad  t-id-yaf  Marius,  ur 
ira ad yemlil yid-s di Utique. Gar-asen si tazwara d tismin akk 
d tuzzma. 
Mi d-yewwev Marius, yekker, yuɣ abrid n ṭṭṛad.  
Si mi iṣeggem lâesker-is, Marius yesdukel wid yellan akk d wid 
i  d-yerna,    yeffeɣ-d  si  Utique,  yezger-d  tilisa,    yebda  tikli  di 
tmurt n Tmazɣa. 
Amennuɣ  mgal  Metellus  yefka-yaɣ-d  abrid  ara  nevfeô  di  tallit 
tamaynut mgal Marius. Di tazwara negguni ad yefreq lâesker-
is. Neooa-ten kecmen-d tamazɣa, teddun iberdan-nsen, beḍḍun 
ɣef  teɣremtin.  Simmal  ferqen,  simmal  tazmert-nsen  tferreq 
ugar.  Yal  tiɣremt    wwven  ad  afen  tiwwura  llint.  Ur  yella 
imenɣi, ur tella tmes, ur  lluéen imezdaɣ-nni, ur rɣant tzeɣwa.  
Nufa abrid-nni yelha. 
Nekk akk d Buxuc, negguni ass-is deg ara nedwi fell-asen. 
Acêal n tikkelt i neɣli ɣef lâesker n Rruman anda ur aɣ-ggunin. 
Snat  tyitwin kan, mi ten-nesduqqes, neqqed kra seg-sen,  ad d 
neffeɣ  seg  wennar.  Nitni  ad  ɣillen  nerwel,  nugad-iten,  nekni  
ad  neddu  deg  webrid-nneɣ  ad  nesduqqes  tarbaât  nniven. 
Akken i asen-nedda acêal n wagguren. D axbacen kan, imenɣi 
ameqqran ur d-yella. Marius nessen-it yeêrec, nekni nunef seg 
webrid-is. 
Tiyita tameqqrant tamezwarut n Marius tusa-aɣ-d si tiɣremt n 
Gafsa. 
D  tikkelt  tamezwarut  i  yedda  lâesker  n  Rruman  deg  webrid 
aɣezfan,  igzem  azaɣar  nekni  ur  nesla.  Nuɣ  tannumi,  di  yal 
tikkelt ara mbiwlen lâeskeô-nsen, nekni ad aɣ-d-yawev wawal. 
Di  yal  tiɣremt,  di  yal  tiɣilt,  di  yal  taqiccuôt,  nesbedd  wid 
yeggunin, wid iéeôôen iberdan uɣen Iôumaniyen.  Anda ddan, 
nekni  nesla.  Tiyita  n  Gafsa  tenser-aɣ.  Marius  mi  yeffeɣ  s 
lâesker-is, yezzi deg webrid, yunef akka d wakka. Mi yewwev 
asif  n  Tanius,  ibeddel  abrid.  Ihegga  tiyelwin  i  waman,  syin 
yeffeɣ  seg  webrid  ameqqran.  Iteddu  deg  yiv,  iteffer  deg  wzal. 
Ur iéri yiwen anida i yella.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Yiwet yiwet armi wwven tawwurt n tiɣremt n Gafsa. 
Mi yewwev Gafsa, iɣli ɣef imezdaɣ n dinna ur bnan ɣef yiman-
nsen. Marius yurar urar-nni n Metellus ass-mi yekcem Begga. 
Mi qrib ad yawev, yezwer imnayen Imaziɣen, wid yellan ddaw 
ufus n Gawda. Mi ten-id-éran at Gafsa nwan d at tmurt s tidet. 
Taggara,  mi  teddun  ad  kecmen,  at  Gafsa  éran-d  ɣer  deffir 
lâeskeô n Rruman. Yekker herwel. 
Akken ad yessekcem tawekka di tmurt-nneɣ, akken ad yeg iɣisi 
ur nselleɣ, Marius yeseêôec Gawda, gma-nni, yerra-t d acengu 
n Tmazɣa. Marius yefka-as lâeskeô, iteddu deg umennuɣ  mgal 
at tmurt-is. Iôeggem-as Marius ad yuɣal d agellid ma yemmut 
Yugurten.    Si  tedyant-nni,  deg  wennar  imenɣi,  tikwal  d  at 
tmurt-iw  i  d  ixûimen.  Sya  d  syin,  d  irgazen  Imaziɣen  i 
yettnaɣen, d idim Amaziɣ i yemmaren. 
At  Gafsa-nni,  lemmer  gan  am  akken  i  asen-nenna,  ad  llin 
tiwwura  n  teɣremt,  nitni  beddlen  tikli.  Mi  d  éran  imnayen  n 
Rruman,  yekker  yimenɣi  mgal  yemnayen-nni  ikecmen  syin 
medlen tiwwura, bedden i tyita mgal wid d iteddun. 
Taggara,  teffeɣ  akken  teffeɣ.  At  Gafsa  ur  zmiren  ad  qablen 
ahdum  n  lâesker  i  yasen-yezzin.  Tiremt  kan,  Iôumaniyen 
hudden ifergan i as-yezzin, kecmen tiɣremt s ujenwi deg ufus. 
Wid  meqqren  nɣan-ten  din,  wiyav  wwin-ten-id  d  aklan.  
Tiɣremt  n  telwit  n  tezdayin  n  tini,  tuɣal-as  d  yir  targit,  ijdi 
amellal yuɣal d azeggaɣ seg yidammen. 
Tiyita-nni  n  Gafsa  tekkes-as  akukru  i  Marius.  Tamurt  yessen-
itt, irgazen llan, yenwa teswa-as-d s wedfel. 
Acemma  kan  deffir  tadyant  n  Gafsa,    Marius  igzem  Tamazɣa  
seg yixef ɣer yixef, ikcem akal yellan tama n wasif n Melwen, 
talast  gar  Nekni  akk  d  tmurt  n  Buxuc.    Din,  iqsed  ad  ikcem 
Tawrirt. 
Tawrirt  tebna  ɣef  weéru  ameqran,  di  tlemmast  uzaɣar.  Yal 
tama  d  acôuf  ur  yezmir  ad  yali  wemdan,  ur  yezmir  yiddew. 
Abrid-is  seg  yiwet  tama  kan  i  yella,  injer  s  ufus  deg  weéru, 
yeḍyeq,  yesuddem ; win imalen deg-s ad yezg deg yiceôfan n 
wadda.  Ifellaêen,  s  yiwen  i  sezriyen  izgaren,  tistan  neɣ 
igemren-nsen.  Amur  ameqqran  bennun-asen  ifergan  deg 
uzaɣar.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Tawrirt d tiɣremt yeddurin am lâec igider. Tama ufella, d awrir 
zun yenjer-it ufus. Di tlemmast n luva-nni tɣez tala.  Imezdaɣ-
is  si  zik  n  zik  ur  yezmir  yiwen  ad  asen-yekcem  tasga.  Sin 
yergazen  zemren  ad  gen  afrag  ɣef  tewwurt  s  ineccaben-nsen. 
Ifellaêen,  yal  ass  ad  adren  akessar,  ad  xedmen  tibêirin  neɣ 
igran-nsen, mi yeɣli yiîij ad alin ɣer tkanna-nsen di Tewrirt. 
Am Metellus di Begga, Am ass-a  Marius di  Tewrirt, yenwa ad 
aɣ-d-yaf dinna, nekk akk d Buxuc, ad yaf agerruj n Tmazɣa, ad 
aɣ-d-yeîîef  s  ufus.  Marius  yezzi  i  Tewrirt,  syin  yessedhem

d-yeçç  tiyita,  ad  yemmet  neɣ  ad  d-yerwel  ɣer  deffir.  Wid 
yessulin  tigejda  i  walluy,  mazal  ttawven  ɣer  yixef  mi  ara  ten-
id-yeçç  ujajiê  n  tmes  neɣ  n  weéru,  ad  grirben  ɣer  deffir.    Yal 
adham ad yawi ɣer lmut  tissi n lâesker n Marius. 
At  Tewrirt  ur  as-gan  aɣilif.  Afrag  yella,  aman  d  wuççi  llan, 
irgazen llan. Yal tikkelt ad grirben Iôumaniyen akessar ad ten-
id-vefrent  teɣratin  n  tlawin.  Marius  yeffeɣ-it  leâqel.  Akken 
yexdem ur as-yufa tawwurt. 
yefra-tt  d  yiman-is,  iteddu  ad  yekkes  lâesker-nni  i  yezzin  i

-  "Ufiɣ  abrid  yessufuɣen  ɣer  tiɣilt  n  Tewrirt.  Lliɣ  leqveɣ

temɣi-d  ɣef  weslav.  Uliɣ  ɣef  tasaft-nni,  ddiɣ  ɣef  ufurk-nni 
yerran  d  asawen  armi  d-ufiɣ  iman-iw  ɣef  tqacuct,  di  Tewrirt

uɣaleɣ akk d wiyav ad sen-mmleɣ abrid !". 
Marius  terkeb-it  tawla.  Iqdef  aâsekriw-nni,  yefka-yas  wid  ɣef 
yettkel, ddan yid-s. Qbel ad alin, kksen taselsa n Rruman, kksen 
uzzal,  lsan  am  Imaziɣen,    ulin  seg  webrid-nni  n  yeârusen, 
wwven  taqacuct-nni  n  Tewrirt.  Mi  d  uɣalen,  d  awal  d-yenna 
umezwaru-nni  i  d-nnan  ineggura-nni.  Abrid  yella.  Marius 
yeffreê. Yufa telli-yas-d tewwurt anda ur yessarem.

Azekka-nni  kan  ihegga  tarbaât,  yerna-asen  lbuq  akken  mi

Gan timecreḍt deg at Tewrirt. Snegren-ten. 
Deffir tedyant-nni n Tewrirt i d-yusa Sulla si Ruma, yewwev-d

Si  tisin-nni  n  Marius  d  Sulla,  kkseɣ  asirem.  Ur  yella  wayen

ṭṭṛad. Tama ad tekk di tayev.  
Asirem  n  talwit  yekkes,  zziɣ-d  tikkelt  nniven  i  tmura.  Awal  i 
asen-nniɣ yiwen : 
- "Ay atmaten ! Aôumani yekcem-d tamurt, Aôumani ilaq-as ad 
yeffeɣ tamurt. D  nitni i d-izegren ilel Agrakal,  maççi d nekni. 
Yiwet tmurt kan i nla. Ur nezmir ad tt-neoo, neɣ ad tt-nefk  d 
tarzeft i Uôumani. Yiwen webrid i yellan ass-a, d abrid n yiseɣ, 
d  abrid  n  tnekra,  ad  nesenger  ajôad  d-ikecmen.  Anida  tufam 
lâesker n Marius, ur din awexxer, ur din inif. Win d-yessutren 
leânaya  eoo-it,  ma  d  wayev  zwi-t  !  Iôumaniyen  i  d-yusan  ad 
sen-neddukel  am  zun  d  aweîîuf.  Ma  s  tubbya  kan  nezmer  ad 
ten-nessenger.  Ay  atmaten !  Ma  teddukel  tcemlit-nneɣ,  ad 
nesergagi  Ruma.  Ass-a  nwen,  azekka  nwen,  tamurt  d  kenwi  i 
tegguni !" 
Mi  d-zziɣ  i  tmurt,  ufiɣ  yuki-d  ugar  uéar-nni  n  tnekra,  uɣeɣ 
abrid ɣer tmurt n Buxuc.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Si  tedyant-nni  mi  nedda  ad  nekcem  Sirta,  teqqim  akken  gar-
aneɣ. Uɣaleɣ ɣur-s akken ad nessemɣer admer ara yessergagin 
Rruman. 
Mi ufiɣ Buxuc, fkiɣ-as tamuɣli-w amek ilaq ad as-neddu i ṭṭṛad 
mgal Rruman. Tamurt yiwet akal yiwen, laûel-nneɣ yiwen, iles 
yiwen.  Nniɣ-as ilaq-aɣ ad nekkes talast yellan gar-aneɣ si tallit 
n  Sifaks,  si  tallit  n  Masensen.  Talast  ibeḍḍun  ad  tt-nekkes,  ad 
nerr  tin  yesduklen,  anda  yebɣa  nekk  qebleɣ.  Nniɣ-as,  Sifaks  d 
jedd-nneɣ,  Masensen  d  jedd-nneɣ.  Ma  nesdukel  iɣallen-nneɣ 
ad  nerr  leqder  i  tmurt-nneɣ.  Ad  nekkes  imennuɣen  gar-aneɣ, 
ad nekkes ayen i aɣ-yebvan ad nesemɣer ayen i aɣ-yesduklen. 
Nniɣ-as  ad  aɣ-zzmen  wid  ara  d-yekkren  azekka  ma  ur  nuɣ 
abrid  n  tdukli.  Ad  aɣ-yezzem  wakal  ɣef  nteddu  ma  nuɣ  yir 
abrid ass-a. Abrid-nneɣ ass-a d abrid n yiseɣ, d abrid n tissas. 
Tikemmict  n  Rruman  i  d  yusan,  ma  neddukel,  ad  tt-nesselfeɣ 
am  tkemmict-nni  n  tizwal.  Aôumani  d-ikecmen  ass-a  tama 
ufella,  ma  yessers  ivaôôen-is,  azekka  ad  yekcem  tama  wadda. 
Aôumani ur yessin ala awal n yiɣil, ala awal n tummeét akk d 
wezduz.  Aôumani  yusa-d  ɣef  tkeckult  n  wesɣar  idegger-itt-id 
wavu  deg  yilel,  azekka  ad  yuɣal  ansi  i  d-yekka,  ad  t-idegger 
wavu n tnekra-nneɣ, abrid-is akin ɣer Ruma. 
Buxuc ifka-yi-d tameééuɣt, yuɣ abrid n jedd-is. 
Nesdukkel  lâesker-nneɣ,  nuɣ  abrid  ɣer  tmurt  anda  yella 
Marius. 
Wid  nesbedd  deg  yiberdan,  deg  yicuqar,    ayen  yellan  ɣef  tiî-
nsen. Anda mbawlen Iôumaniyen, ad aɣ-d-yawev wawal. 
Mi  nella  nteddu  deg  webrid  i  d-nemlal  amnay  s  wegmer-is 
iteddu-d  s  tazzla.    Isalan  i  yaɣ-d-yewwi  sfeôêen-aɣ  :  "Marius 
akk  d  lâesker-is  llan  teddun  di  tzaɣart  yellan  akin  zdat,  deffir  
yiɣil". 
Niqal ad neddu acêal n wagguren ara ntezzi si tmurt ɣer tmurt 
akken  ad  d-naf  lateô  n  Marius,  taggara  yeɣli-d  netta  deg 
webrid-nneɣ. 
Din,  nbeddel  tikli,  nefka  imnayen  zwaren  ɣer  zdat  ad  aɣ-d- 
awin  isalan  n  wanda  llan,  acêal  i  yellan,  anwa  abrid  deg 
teddun.  Nekk  d  Buxuc  nesemlal-d  ifesyanen-nneɣ  ad  nheggi 
tiyita.  Nteddu, nferru-tent amek ara as-neddu i yimenɣi mgal 
Marius.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Yebda iɣelli wass mi nemlal Marius d lâeskeô-is deg yelmaten. 
Tamurt nekni nessen-itt, d azal neɣ d iv, irgazen-nneɣ zemren 
ad nnaɣen akken ran. Nebla ma nezzi nefka tissi tamezwarut n 
yemnayen  teɣli fella-asen  am  tmedda. Qbel ad rren tiyita, mi 
llan  tezzin  akken  ad  gen  afrag  yezzin,  nekni  nerna  tissitin  n 
yergazen nniven. Yekker uhetwir, nekni nekkat, nitni kkaten. 
Tiî-nneɣ nekni ad asen-nezzi, ad sen-neg tasraft anda yiwen ur  
d-iteffeɣ.  Nek  sya,  Buxuc  syin,  tekker  tɣebbart,  simmal 
nessiḍyiq annar, simmal néeô nferrez anda nekkat. S terbaât n 
yemnayen  yellan  yid-i,    kecmeɣ  di  tlemmast  akken  ad  awveɣ 
Marius,  nekni  nekkat,  nitni  êebbken  akken  ad  snesren  iman-
nsen. Ajenwi yedda, timseggeft tedda, aneccab yedda. Yal tama 
tekkat, tettazzal, tnehhet, nettuɣu, tekker tɣebbaôt, irgazen wa 
ibedd  ɣef  ivarren-is,  wa  yesred  am  uceîîiv.    Yal  tikkelt  mi 
wwteɣ  ad  qerbeɣ  anda  nwiɣ  yella  Marius,    taggara  tiyita, 
adham  n  yemnayen  ad  aɣ-d-rren  ɣer  deffir,  ad  aɣ-sinfen  ɣer 
yeffus neɣ zelmev. 
Imenɣi yeêma, iîij yebda iɣelli, irgazen-nneɣ am izmawen. 
Acemma  kan  tenɣes  tyita,  Iôumaniyen  bdan  nesren  d  tidist. 
Agus-nni i asen-nhegga ur yeîîif, Marius akk d kra n lâesker-is 
nesren,  syin  uɣen  amkan  deg  yiwen  wegni,  yufrar-d  asawen. 
Ger  iôumaniyen-nni,  win  snesren  ivaôôen-is  yenser,  wayev 
yečča-t uneccab neɣ ajenwi. 
Lâeskeô  n  Rruman,  ɣas  éran  maççi  ɣef  tmurt-nsen  i  kkaten, 
maççi  d  akal-nsen  i  ɣef  ttnaɣen,  nitni  ssnen-as  i  yimenɣi. 
Tussna imenɣi lemden-tt, rnan ttaɣen awal ugar. Akken i asen-
yenna  ufesyan  ad  aɣen  abrid-is.  Marius  yezwar-asen  ɣer 
wegni-nni,  nitni  ddan  di  later-is,  teddun  kkaten-d  ɣer  deffir,  
nekni nedda deg yivaôôen-nsen. Iv yeɣli-d, imenɣi yefra. 
Nefra abrid-is nekk akk d Buxuc.  Skud tella taffza, nezzi-as-d s 
lâesker  i wegni zun d taxatemt.  Ur  tella tardast nezgel,  yiwen 
uâsekriw n Rruman ur yezmir ad yeffeɣ syin, awtul ur yezmir 
ad yenser. 
Nemsefham  nekk  d  Buxuc  i  tyita  mi  ara  ad  yali  wass.    Ansi 
wenten ad d ffɣen Iôumaniyen, nekni ad ten-nesni d asnay.  Mi 
nemsefraq,  yal  wa  yerra  anda  llan  lâesker-is.    Neéra  ad  yiɣzif 
yiv.

Akken  sersen  iman-nsen  Imaziɣen-nneɣ,  ssaɣen  iêeoouoa  n 
tmes,  dɣa kkren i wbendir d lɣiva. Tarewla-nni yerwel lâesker 
n Rruman yeffer, ɣillen dayen yefra imenɣi. Abendir yeêma seg 
tyita,  maççi  d  ayen  ara  tessusmev.    Atmaten-nneɣ  smeɣren 
adriz, afus yekkat, tiqesôit tekkat tadersit.  Mi nella nesseêmay 
adriz, nnig-nneɣ Marius akk d lâesker-is xemten, ur yella ûûut, 
ur yella wawal, ssusmen am zun mmuten. 
Mi  yedda  yiv,  Imaziɣen-nneɣ  feclen,  ssusmen,  win  yeâyan  ad 
isers  iman-is  ad  igen  gar  watmaten-is,  armi  d-ters  tsusmi. 
Gran-d iâessasen bedden akin. 
Lawan-nni kan deg âziz yives, atmaten-nneɣ élen, imir i yesker 
aɣebbar Marius akk d lâesker-is. Di tlemmast n yiv i d-heggan 
iman-nsen  ad  nesren.  Uɣen-d  takessart  d  adham,  s  tazzla  d 
usuɣu,  lbuq  yekkat,  ajenwi  yekkat,  aneccab  yekkat.  Mazal  d 
nseggem  iman-nneɣ  i  tyita,  nitni  zrin  akin,  nesren  i  tcebbakt- 
nni i asen-nga. Win nɣan nɣan-t, win rekven rekven-t. Marius 
yenser i lmut. 
Sduqsen-aɣ  asduqqes-nni  yelhan.  Anda  ilaq  d  nekni  ara  ten- 
yesduqqsen  acemma  kan  qbel  ad  yali  wass,  Marius  yugar-aɣ 
tiêerci, yezwar talalit n wass. 
Timlilit  n  Yelmaten  tefka-aɣ-d  udem  n  yimenɣi.  Marius  i  d 
neîîef gar ifassen-nneɣ, inser-aɣ s tmussni-s, s tiêḥerci n ṭṭṛad. 
Ger  wid  ukud  nennuɣ,  icban  Bestia,  Albinus  neɣ  Metelllus,  
ɣur-i  Marius  yerna  adar  s  tmussni  n  ṭṭṛad.  Ma  zik  imenɣi  d 
adrar, ass-a d igenni. Akken i as-nekka i tedyant-nni nekk akk 
d Buxuc ur as-nufa ixef-is. Amek i nettwakellex akken ? Amek 
i aɣ-tenser ?  Neçça-tt teêma. 
Ur  tella  din  teɣzef  n  wawal.    Akken  i  aɣ-yekkes  uzaylal-nni, 
nserreo, nedda deffir Marius d lâesker-is. 
Marius iteddu, nekni nedda di lateô-is. Uvan ussan nteddu deg 
webrid-is. Abrid n Marius iteddu ɣer Sirta. Ass wis ôebâa neɣli 
fella-asen.

ihegga.

yergazen  s  ineccaben  neɣ  s  ijenwiyen.  Iôumaniyen  zzin,

Marius  ikemmel  abrid-is  akin,  deg  webrid  n  Sirta,    Buxuc33 
yesdukel lâesker-is, yeîîef yiwet tiɣilt akin, nekni neqqim din ad 
nenîel irgazen-nneɣ.  Neqqim ad as-nesefru i tedyant yevran. 
Tagrest  tusa-d,  Marius  yuli  akin  ɣer  tama  n  Carthage,  yerna 
yesdukel lâesker-is di teɣremtin îîfen di Tmazɣa, yecban Sirta, 
Zama. Buxuc yuɣal ɣer wexxam-is, nekk uɣaleɣ i tazzla akken 
ad  d-snekreɣ  tamurt  d  amaynut  i  Marius.  Ma  yella  ccek, 
aneggaru-yagi  yesban-d  anda  i  tent-nuɣ.  Nuɣ-itent  di  tuddsa.

dwin  akka  d  wakka,  zun  ɣer  tesvav  n  wewtul  neɣ  n  yilfan. 
Adway-nni  ur  yella  d  abrid.  Ilaq-aɣ  ad  nernu  aselmed  ugar  i

neqqim.

netturar ɣef teblavin. Yal alqaf yeddukel akk d wid yezwaren, 
yerna  ihegga  tiyita  i  yelqafen  d-iteddun.  Tuddsa  Tevres, 
temcuddal. 
Imenɣi mgal Rruman friɣ-tt, ad as-nbeddel abrid. 
Ilaq-aɣ ad as-neqqim skud ur  nhegga  lâesker am  akken  i  ten-
ihegga Rruman. Tiyita n Yelmaten, tin n Sirta fkant-aɣ-d talast 
yellan gar-aɣ d Rruman. Tidet, ɣas îîfen tiɣremtin, zzin agadir 
d afrag, tamurt d nekni i tt-yeîîfen. £as ad nanef i yimenɣiyen 
imeqqranen,  ansi  kkan  ad  aɣ-d-afen  zdat-nsen,  yal  takemmict 
n lâesker-nsen i d-yeffɣen si teɣremt  ad tenger, anida kkan ad 
afen  tasraft  deg  webrid-nsen.  Ad  asen-neddu  s  tyita  n  tuqqsa, 
am tuqqsa n waôeé. 
Akka  i  as-ddiɣ.  Mi  nefra  nekk  akk  d  yifesyanen-nneɣ,  yal 
tarbaât tuɣ abrid-is. I yal tiɣmert n tmurt  ad nessiwev awal, ad 
nessiwev asirem i tnekra yugaren tin yezrin.

Di  tallit-nni  deg  lliɣ  tedduɣ  deg  yiberdan,  ôwiɣ  akessar  d

Ayen i ɣezzif wawal yelha. 
Ass-mi  ériɣ  Buxuc,  nniɣ-as  ad  iyi-d-yefk  amek  yessedda  awal

tseɣlev  wwet  ;  ma  ur  tezmirev  ur  sɣal »  ,  nekni  nekker-d,

acengu-nneɣ.  Ma zemreɣ ad ssinfeɣ tallit-a deg nella ɣer tifrat,

Ayen  riɣ  ad  as-skecmeɣ  i  Buxuc  ɣer  wallaɣ-is :  d  tikerkas, 
tiêeôci n Marius akk d ifesyanen-is. Nekk ɣur-i tamsalt teqqen, 
tefra-d  si  Ruma.  Marius  fkan-t-id  ad  iseddu  ṭṭṛad,  netta  ad 
yewwet  s  wayen  yezmer  akken  ad  yawev  iswi-s  :  Rruman  ad 
yeîîef Tamazɣa. 
Ayen nniven akk d urar, d tuzya n wawal. Takti yagi tekcem-
iyi  ɣer  wallaɣ-iw  ur  zmireɣ  ad  tt-id-ssuffɣeɣ.  Awal  n  Rruman 
yebna ɣef tkerkas, ur yella din wawal n tidet. 
Atmaten-nneɣ  i  yellan  di  tmurt  n  Carthage,  di  Utique, 
ṣṣawven-aɣ-d  awal.    Marius  simmal  yessekcam-d  lâesker 
irennu-d, si Ruma.  Win yessarmen talwit, ur d-irennu  iɣallen 
d ifadden n ṭṭṛad. 
Di lawan deg Buxuc yesselqam awal netta d Sulla, nekk lhiɣ-d 
di  tfellaêt-iw.  Yal  ass  anda  ara  yeɣli  yis-neɣ.    Nejjem  ad  nens 
sin wuvan deg yiwem wemkan. Nedda d timzizzelt, yal tiɣremt 
nekcem  yiwen  wudem  i  nufa.  Imdanen  bedden,  heggan  i 
tnekra,  kkren  i  twizi  mgal  Aôumani.  £as  irgazen  llan,  ɣas 
idamen  êman,    amur  ameqran  d  ifellaêen.  Ifassen    yuɣen 
tannumi d uqabac akk d wanzel, ur zmiren azekka-nni kan ad 
ṣegmen  i  uneccab,  axtuc  neɣ  ajenwi.    Ur  zmireɣ  ad  megreɣ 
irgazen di tmura, ad ten-fkeɣ d asfel i ujenwi n Rruman. Abrid-
iw  nekk,  yal  ilemzi-nneɣ,  ilaq-as  ad  yekcem  ɣer  wennar 
imenɣi, ad yewwet, syin ad yeffeɣ d ameddur.  Riɣ ad ilin d wid 
ara yewwten, maççi d wid a yemten. 
Zegreɣ asif n Melwen, kecmeɣ tamurt n Buxuc. Yuzen-d ɣur-i 
ad  t-zreɣ.  Mi  nemlal,  yefka-yi-d  anda  yessawev  awal  gar-as  d 
Marius.  Netta  yessarem  ad  naf  tawwurt  i  tifrat.  Yenna-yi-d :  
« Iôumaniyen  fkan-d  udem  akken  yal  yiwen  ad  yaɣ  abrid  n 
telwit ; ma neqqim, nezmer ad nefru uguren yellan gar-aneɣ ; 
ma neqqim-as, ur tella tindert ur nfessi ». 
Taggara,  buxuc  isegra-d  awal,  yenna-yi-d  :"Marius  yuzen-d 
Sulla    ad  nemlil  yid-s.  Abrid  n  tifrat  ad  t-id-naf  akken  yebɣu 
yentel.  Keçč  a  Yugurten,  ilaq-ak  ad  tôedbev,  ad  tefsiv  tundar,  
ad d-tefkev udem akken ad nekkes tazzla idammen gar-aneɣ d 
Rruman." 
Awal n Buxuc s webrid-is. Acu tettnadiv ay aderɣal, d tafat !

Nekk,  s  tidet,  walaɣ  awal-nni  d  uffal.  Ayen  ur  d-yessefreé 
Buxuc, nekk ɣur-i d tagejdit n wawal. Ma yella isawel netta d 
Sulla,  awal  amezwaru  d  wa  :  Iôumaniyen  ad  ffɣen  si  Tmazɣa,

simmal trennu teddal awal-is. Nekk, tiêerci n Marius ssneɣ-tt,

-  Nekni  akk  d  Rruman  am  tedyant-nni  "mmi-s  n  taɣaḍt  ad  t-
yeçç wuccen".  Sulla yenna-ak ad yas. Nekk, yiwen webrid kan 
i  walaɣ  yessuffuɣ.  Sulla  ad  t-id-neîîef  gar  ifassen-nneɣ,  syin 
Iôumaniyen ad fken udem, am Marius am Senat di Ruma. Ma

nneɣ. Buxuc idhec. Abrid i as-d-wwiɣ ur yebni fell-as. Ur iyi-d-

netta d Sulla. Nefra ad yerr ɣuri kra wussan ɣer zdat. 
Timlilit-nni n Buxuc ur tris ɣef nniyya-w. Awal iyi-d-yessawev 
Dabeô,  win  yellan  tama-s,  qbel  timlilit-agi  n  Buxuc  akk  d

Tamazɣa  d  Muriṭanya.  Nuɣ  abrid  nekk  akk  d  terbaât,  yid-neɣ 
ddan  sin  warraw-iw.  Mi  qrib  ad    nawev,  neéra  s  lbaâd 
aveggal-iw Buxuc, ibedd ɣef yixef n tiɣilt netta d yimnayen-is. 
Yezger-d  i  wasif  akken  ad  aɣ-dyemmager.  Nekni  nesɣel-as, 
netta  yesɣel-aɣ-d  s  yiɣil-is.  Mi  nerna  tikli  ad  neddu  ɣer  zdat, 
qbel ad ten-nawev i d ɣlin fell-aɣ. yezzi-yaɣ-d weglaf n lâesker 
n Rruman.  Llan neṭlen  i tmuɣli, akin ddaw udernu. 
Nekni  nella  ifassen-nneɣ  d  ilmawen.  Ur  yella  s  wayes  ara

akk d sin warraw-iw. Qqnen-aɣ tixelxalin n wuzzal.

- 3 - 
Tikli n Ruma34 

 
 
 
 
 

 
 

D tannumi n Rruman : yal argaz ara yesmeɣren tamurt-
nsen  akin  i  tlisa  yellan,  nitni  ad  as-gen  tameɣra  tameqqrant 
(Triumphum) di tlemmast n Ruma. 
Tameɣra-nni deg-s sin wudmawen, tebrek temlel : d tameɣra i 
at  Ruma,  d  tanîelt  i  wid  yettwarzen,  cudden  s  txelxalin  n 
wuzzal, ddan di tlemmast n lâeskeô. 
Ussan n tegrest  yezdeɣ-iten usemmiv. 
Tewzel  n  wussan-nni  trennu  amur  i  teɣzi  n  wuvan  akken  ad 
sebken idammen, ad yeqqar weglim, ad kkawen ifadden. 
Asemmiv n Ruma yeqseê, di tegrest yerna tardast ɣer zdat. 
Campus Martius35, agni-nni yellan di tlemmast n Ruma, deffir 
ugadir,    yeççuô  d  imdanen,  yeççur  d  igemren,  d  izgaren  seg 
wacêal  n  wussan  aya.  Imezdaɣ-nni  n  Campus  Martius  d 

                                                            
34 Dans la Rome Antique, le Triomphe (Triumphum), c'est  la procession accomplie 
au  temple  de  Jupiter  Capitolinus  par  un  général  vainqueur.  …  le  triomphateur 
richement vêtu et couronné de lauriers, traversait la ville montée sur un char attelé 
de  quatre  chevaux  blancs.  L'armée  criait  "io  triumphe"  et  chantait  des  chansons 
paillardes. Suivaient les membres du Sénat, les magistrats, les prisonniers, le butin 
et les animaux destinés au sacrifice. Le cortège partait du Champ de Mars, hors les 
murs, entrait dans Rome par la porte triomphale, traversait le Circus maximus, 
contournait  le  Palatin,  avant  d'emprunter  la  Voie  sacrée  pour  atteindre  le 
Capitole.  Parvenu  au  Temple  de  Jupiter,  le  général  immolait  lui-même  les 
animaux destinés aux sacrifices et offrait sa couronne de lauriers au dieu.... 
Ce défilé était attribué par le Sénat romain, et constituait une récompense pour le 
général  victorieux.  Il  pouvait  avoir  lieu  longtemps  après  sa  campagne.  Un  des 
critères  importants  était  le  butin  rapporté,  mais  il  ne  pouvait  y  avoir  de 
triomphe  si  l'ager  romanus,  le  territoire  de  la  République,  n'avait  pas  été 
augmenté. 
35 Campus Martius  (Champ de Mars) / Annar n Meɣres, beôôa ugadir n Ruma.
