imezdaɣ  n  tmara.  Ur  llan  d  wid  yetturaren,  ur  llan  d  wid  d-
yusan  ad  nezhen  uraren  n  circus  Flaminius  neɣ  circus 
Maximus,  deffir  tawant,  deffir  uççi  yelhan  akk  d  tissit  n 
waman n wavil. Imdanen-nni qqimen d tikemmucin, ssusmen,  
lâesker  n  Rruman  itezzi-asen,  teddun  akka  d  wakka,  afus  ɣef 
ujenwi neɣ uneccab. 
Urar deg wennar n Campus Martius di tegrest useggas -104 ur 
yella  d  win  ssnen  akk  imezdaɣ  n  Ruma.  Urar-nni  i  yasen-d-
ihegga Consul Marius i at Ruma, ira ad yili d win ɣef ara cfun 
iseggasen  d  iseggasen,  d  win  ara  êekkun  yemdanen  i  tarwa- 
nsen, i warraw n warraw-nsen, si lqern ɣer lqern. Akken i t ira 
Marius. 
Acêal  n  wussan  si  mi  yeççuô  wennar  n  Campus  Martius.  Yal 
ass  rennun-d  yemdanen,  igemren,  izgaren.  Mi  d-tekcem  tissi 
ad taɣ amkan-is akin di teɣmert i as-heggan lâeskeô-nni. 
Tasusmi n wennar-nni trennu aɣilif ugar i wemkan-nni. Taduli 
n  tigugemt  tewwev  ula  d  izgaren  akk  d  iserdan-nni.  Üṣut  i  d 
yulin si Campus nni, tikwal d win kan n lâesker-nni i yezzin i 
wegraw,  neɣ  d  astenten  n  txelxalin  n  wuzzal.  Tixelxalin-nni 
yurzen irgazen wa ɣer wayev. Asemmiv-nni n tegrest n Öuma 
yesberber-asen, yesdukel imdanen-nni, idel taduli n tsusmi fell-
asen. 
Acêal  n  wussan  si  mi  yeççur  wennar-nni.  Laé  d  uṣemmiv 
kecmen  iɣsan  n  yemdanen.  Tiɣimit-nni  n  yal  ass,  si  tsebêit  ar 
tmeddit,  si  tmeddit  ar  tsebêit,  tessekref-iten,  laé  d  usemmiv 
yerna-yasen. Qqimen feclen. 
£as serden,  ur uysen, ssarmen ad tbeddel fell-asen, am akken 
nnan  imezwura :  "akken  triv  ɣezzifev  a  yiv,  taggara  ad  yali 
wass". Tikwal dɣa ssaramen ad yas wass deg ara tefru fell-asen, 
ad yeffeɣ yiîij, ad yekkes uɣemɣum-nni deg llan. Melmi ara d-
yas wass ssaramen ? 
Imdanen-nni yeqqnen am wakraren ur llan d imezdaɣ n Ruma, 
ur  llan  d  imezdaɣ  n  Latinium,  n  Liguria,  neɣ  n  tmura  n 
Rruman  i  d  yezzin  akin.  Nitni  usan-d  si  tmurt  yellan  akin  i 
yilel, akin i waman izegzawen. Usan-d nnig lebɣi-nsen, ur llan 
d inebgawen n Ruma.

Ëemmu,  zzin-aɣ,  îîfen-aɣ,  fkan-aɣ  ayen  i  umi  zemren  n  tyita,

Yal  yiwen  tadyant  i  d  yeêka,  yal  wa  d  aɣilif  i  t-yecqan  ;  wa

Imdanen  qqimen,  qqumcen,  ggunin,  tiddi  ur  tella.  D  amured 
kan  di  snat  turdas-nni  deg  llan  i  ubeddel  n  tmeûûaḍt.  Win

tama ɣer tayev, mmuten din. Wid d yegran kerfen, uɣalen ɣef 
tgecrar.  Ifen-ten  igemren-nni  d  yezgaren-nni  izeggaɣen  d 
imellalen, nitni meqqar zemren ad qimen, ad bedden. 
Yir  rriêa  tuɣ  akk  annar.  Ger  tuffɣa  n  yemdanen  akk  d  tin  n 
waxfiwen,  tazefrant-nni  trennu  teqseê  yal  ass.  Lâesker  n 
Rruman  simmal  rennun  teddun  akin,  simmal  rewwlen  akin, 
ɣunfan rriêa n yemdanen-nni, rriêa n wufni.  
Acêal d ussan i yezrin, imdanen-nni ggunin tafat ansi ara sen-
d-tas. Deg wass amcum, qbel ad yali wass i yekker herwel deg 
wennar Martius. 
Asuɣu-nni  n  lâeskeô  n  Rruman  ad  yessaki  win  yemmuten. 
Teddun, afus yekkat, iêebbek  akka d wakka, win yeqqimen ad 
yekker,  win  yemmuten  ad  yekker,  win  ur  nezmir  ad  t-yeçç 
ujajiê. Akken llan  yemdanen-nni neggzen, bedden nnig lebɣi-
nsen.  Bedden  yir  tiddi  deffir  acêal  n  wussan  n    uqummec,  n 
tikerfi.  Tagecrirt  tenṭeq,  taweîzit  tsuɣ,  tiqesrit  tsuɣ.  Win 
yewwten  ad  yeqqim,  din  ara  t-id-tawev  tyita  n  wanzel  n 
Rruman. Ur tella tasa, ur yella yillu. 
Si  teqreê-nni  n  zellum  usemmiv,  iɣsan  saêen,  igelman 
ddubzen,  tiddi  n  yemdanen-nni  tmal,  tekna  am  terga  uɣanim 
deg wass n wavu.

rennun adar zdat wayev. Yuli wass mi bdan tikli. Teddun tikli

Wid  yellan  seg-sen  ssnen  Ruma,  éôan  zdat-sen  Circus

Afrag ineccaben n lâesker-nni si yal tama yeksa fell-asen aɣilif.

ggunint twuɣa, ur ten-yegguni waêêay !

Acêal n tikkal i yezger ilel, yerzef ɣer Ruma. Dɣa si tedyant-nni

nni, dɣa at Ruma bdan-d yir awalen ɣer wudem-is.

Isers  aqerruy-is,  ur  isel  i  yir  awal,  ur  yuki  i  tsusaf-nni  i  t-id-

iban-as-d  am  tafat-nni  n  magu,  iban-as  yefren,  yufaf,  yektal, 
yuɣal  ɣer  tesga.  Triumphum  agi  iban-as-d  am  win  yufan 
tasarut-nni i as-idergen acêal n wussan, acêal n yiseggasen. 
Azal  ameqqran  n  Triumphum yessen-it  netta.  Yeéra  anwa  i  d 
aéar-is di tmurt n Rruman : akken ad ttili tikli n Triumphum i 
yiwen  seg  wid  yeseddan  ṭṭṛad,  i  jiniral  n  lâesker  i  yecban 
Marius,  ilaq  cceôt  ameqqran.  Ilaq-as  ad  yili  yerna-d  akal39 
akken ad yessemɣer, ad yessnerni tamurt n Rruman. 
Senat i as-d-iqeblen ass-a tikli-agi n Triumphum i Marius, ɣur-
s tefra. Marius yerna-d tamurt i Rruman, idegger akin tilisa n 
tmurt  n  Rruman,  yerna-d  Tamazɣa  (Numidya)  d  aêric 
amaynut  i  Ruma.  £ur-sen  tefra,  seg  wass-nni  deg  d-îîfen 
Yugurten,  Tamazɣa tuɣal d taferka-nsen. 
Afrag-nni  iga  Yugurten  yekkes-asen  i  Rruman  seg  wass-mi  t-
id-cudden s ixelxalen n wuzzal ! 
Yugurten iteddu, avar deffir wayev, ur yesla i twuɣa, ur yuki i 
tsusaf. Aɣilif-nni ameqqran yellan fell-as yuki-as yettifsus. Ass-
a tefra-as-d. Anezgum-nni iga seg wass-mi yekker i ṭṭṛad mgal 
Rruman,  ass-a  yettifrir  am  tagut-nni  n  tefsut.  Akukru-nni  
yemmugger  acêal  d  tallit,  di  yal  imenɣi,    ass-a  yekkes.  Yeéra 
netta seg wass amezwaru deg webrid n tissas i yella.  Yennuɣ 
Rruman  acku  nitni  begsen  di  tazwara  ad  kecmen  Tamazɣa. 
Tamettant-nni  n  Makawsen  tusa-asen-d  d  tawwurt  akken  ad 
kecmen Sirta. Nitni heggan, begsen, cudden-tt, taggara ufan-d 
Yugurten d axsim-nsen. 
Abrid-nni  heggan-t  si  zik.  Heggan  arraw  n  Makawsen  akken 
ad  kerzen  yis-sen.  Lemmer  ur  ten-heggan  yili  Aderbal  ur  d 
yessuffuɣ  awalen-nni  zdat  tejmaât  n  Senat  ass-mi  yezger  ɣer 
Ruma akken ad yeccetki. Yenna-yasen ass-nni : "Tamurt d ayla-
nwen kenwi, nekni d iqeddacen-nwen ...". 
Afus deg-neɣ i yella. 

                                                            
39  Triomphe : " Un des critères importants était le butin rapporté, mais il ne pouvait 
y avoir de triomphe si l'ager romanus, le territoire de la République, n'avait pas été 
augmenté".  L’annexion de la Numidie se confirme !

Di  15  yiseggasen  imenɣi  mgal  Rruman,  llant  tikwal  anda 
Yugurten    iga  ccek.  Llant  tikwal  i  deg  yefcel.  Taggara,  yal 
tikkelt yettaf tazmert ɣer zdat, yettaf afud amaynut i tnekra. 
Yugurten  iteddu  s  taéeyt,  knant  tuyat,    ger  tiwuɣa  d  uqejjem, 
allaɣ-is yunag akin ɣer wedrar n Awras, akin ɣer Sirta. 
Mi  d-yetkaki  ilmeéiyen-nni  i  d-yemmugger  di  tikli-s  di  yal 
tiɣremt  n  Tmazɣa,  yeéra  deg  wul-is  ass-a,  yeééa  di  tmurt-is 
aéar n tnekra. 
Yeéôa  yessaɣ  tafat  n  tnekra  deg  wulawen-nsen.  Tafat-nni  ur 
nxessi. Yeqqen allen-is, iteddu am uderɣal, avar deffir wayev. 
£er zdat, Marius, s ufella ucaôiv amellal i jebdent snat tyugwin 
igemren  imellalen,  iteddu  ɣer  tewrirt  n  Capitolinus.  Iteddu 
akken  ad  yefk  lwaâda,  ad  yeééal,  ad  yessizzel  idammen  i 
Jupiter. Ad as-yerr lxiô…

- 4 - 
Di Tullianum 

 
 
 
 
 

 
 

Mi  tewwev  tikli  n  triomphe  ɣer  Capitolinus,  Marius 
yeééul taéallit-is,  yessazzel idammen n yezgaren at wacciwen.  
Yewwev lebɣi-s. 
Imeêbas  Imaziɣen  akk  d  wid  n  tmura  nniven,  nehôen-ten  ɣer 
iderbaz anda ttilin. Azekka-nsen yiwen, d aberkan : ad nzen d 
aklan-neɣ ad ten-yeçç ujenwi neɣ yizem deg wuraren n circus 
di Ṛuman. Ffɣen si tudert. 
Yugurten ssudren-t ɣer lêebs Mamertinum, d abrid ɣer tesraft 
n Tullianum, akin ddaw tewrirt n Capitolinus, deg yixef n Via 
sacra. 
Qbel  ad  gren  Yugurten  deg  yimi40  ufella  n  tesfrat-nni,  fsin-as 
tixelxalin-nni n wuzzal, kksen-as iceṭṭiven-is, rnan jerêen-t mi 
as-d-qeccmen timengucin-nni n wureɣ seg yimeééuɣen-is. 
Inîer ɣer tlemmast n tesraft tasemmaḍt, d aâeryan akken i t-id-
turew  yemma-s.  Yenîeô  ɣef  yeblaven,  imeééuɣen  teddun  d 
idammen...  
 
I ɣezzifev a yiv ! 
Tillas d usemmiv zedɣen tasraft-nni deg yekcem Yugurten. 
Tebrek  akk  d  yir  rriêa  rennunt-as  ugar  aɣilif  i  wemviq-nni. 
Tasraft-nni  telli-d  imi-s  si  ddaw  tmurt  am  zun  d  talafsa.  Ur 
yuki mi d yufa iman-is yeglalez adda, di tlemmast n tesraft. Mi 
as-d-bran si tama ufella, ur yeéra yeɣli-d ɣef uqerru-s neɣ ɣef 
ivaôôen-is. Yeqqim, yenzef.

Rriêa-nni i t-id-yewwten ɣer tanzarin-is, tesmektay-as-d ifran-
nni  n  Taza,  ifran-nni  anda  zedɣen  yizmawen.  Yugurten 
yeccarrew.  yeééel afus-is, yufa-t ééay zun d azduz. £as kksent 
txelxalin  n  wuzzal  i  t-yurzen  acêal  n  wagguren,  yuki-as  i 
tesmev-nni-nsent, yuki-as i taéeyt-nni-nsent. Yemmekta-d anda 
yella. 
Akken yeqqim ur as-yufa udem. 
Teqseê-d  tesmev  n  yeblaven-nni  gan-as-d  ineccaben  deg 
weksum-is. Yeééel ivaôôen-is, yufa yerra-t-id udernu n weéru.  
Tigecrar qqiment kerfent. Iṣeggem iman-is. 
Ur yeéôa llint wallen-is neɣ qqnent. Ur yeéra amek i as-d-tegra 
i yeéri-s.  Ur yeéri d ass neɣ d iv, tezzint deg wallaɣ-is. Tebrek-
nni  n  tesraft  akk  d  tillas-nni  rnant  tidderɣelt  i  tidderɣelt. 
Yeqqim, yessusem. 
Yuki-yas  i  tesmev  tuɣ  aglim-is.  Isers  afus-is  ɣef  yedmaren-is, 
yufa  ur  yella  uceṭṭiv,  ur  tella  tselsa.  Yegra-d  akken  d  ilul  si 
tâebbuḍt n yemma-s. 
Yesself i wudem-is, yuki i ufus-is yulwaɣ, yeêma-d si tnalit-nni. 
Idammen  rennun  tazla  seg  yimeééuɣen-is,  udren-d  d  akessar, 
gan-d targa ɣer tuyat-is. 
Yugurten yewwet ad yetkaki. Acêal aya  i  yella di  tesraft-agi ? 
Imir kan ? D ussan, neɣ d aguren ? 
Ur d yufa. Xeôbent deg wallaɣ-is. 
Rriêa-nni  tazefrant  n  tesraft  terna  tɣeééa-t  ugar  di  tenzert-is. 
Rriêa-nni  tesmekta-as-d  tadyant-nni,  ass-mi  yevfer  izem  nepa 
d yimeddukal-is, Ameqqran akk d Gider, di teégi n Taza, tiégi n 
wegdel deg wedrar n Awras. 
Yugurten  yetkaki  d  tedyant-nni,  iéeô-itt,  zun  tella-d  zdat 
waîîiwen-is : 
-  "  ...  mi  aɣ-yenser  yizem-nni  tikkelt  tamezwarut,  neooa  din 
imeddukal,    wid  yeddan  yid-neɣ.  Nuzzel,  nuɣ  abrid  deg  yezri 
yizem-nni. Nedda acêal, izem yufeg, yucka, ur d-iban lateô-is. 
Nezzi  i  teégi,  nekka-as  tama  ufella,  nerna  tama  n  wadda,  ur 
yella  yizem.  Nerna  tikli  ɣer  zdat,  syin  ners  ɣer  tmurt.  Neqqen 
igemren-nneɣ dɣa nedda ɣef  uvar  gar  yisekla n wegdel akk d 
umadaɣ. 
Mi  nuli  asawen,  newwev  ɣer  yiwen  weslav,  nufa  dinna  llan 
iceôfan, llan yefran. Negguni  tiremt,  ur  d  yenṭiq wefôux, ur d

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

ineggez wewtul. Tasusmi-nni tdel amviq-nni, tesberber-as zun 
d tasusmi-nni usalu n wedfel yessan. 
Ameqqran  akk  d  Gider  zzin-d  s-wadda,  nekk  lliɣ  tama  ufella. 
èôiɣ-ten mi bedden akin. Sseɣleɣ-asen s uneccab-inu akken ad 
asen-iniɣ : "nekk ad kecmeɣ ɣer yefri-nni yellan zdat-i, nitni ad 
bedden ɣef yiman-nsen". 
Gider  yerra-yi-d  s  yiɣil-is,  zun  akken  yenna-d  :  "keçč  zwir, 
nekni  ad  nergel  abrid  n  wadda".    Ddiɣ  snat  tsuraf  kan  gar 
yeblaven mi ɣliɣ ɣef yimi n yefri. Amruj-nni n yifri yella yeffer-
it udafal,yevres fell-as am zun d azeîîa. 
Yella deg wawal : "ifri n yizem, ɣas d ilem yessagad". 
Mi skecmeɣ aqerruy-iw di tewwurt n yifri iyi-d-tewwet rriêa-
nni  ɣer  tenzarin-iw,  rriêa-nni  taqesêant,  tazefrant.  Mi  d-rriɣ 
iman-iw ɣer deffir akken ad nefseɣ abeêri azedgan i d-ineggez 
kra zdat-i, yeffeɣ-d ger igenni akk tmurt, yufeg akin am wavu 
ɣer  tama  n  teégi.  Imir,  nekk  ur  ériɣ  tigert.  Ukiɣ  kan  i  wavu 
ameqran,  « huuufff ! Ukiɣ  i  kra  ihucc-iyi  akin,  icrew  iɣil-iw, 
syin ivegger-iyi akin ɣer weslav n tnicca. 
Mi d ukiɣ, ufiɣ-d iman-iw éleɣ ger yimeddukal-iw, Gider akk d 
Ameqqran,  aqerruy-iw  icudd  s  uceṭṭiv  n  tejbirt  umagraman. 
Mi  serseɣ  afus-iw  ɣef  uqerruy-iw,  ukiɣ  i  êamu  n  idammen-
nni...". 
Tesmev-nni  n  tesraft  tebda  tkeççem  ugar  deg  yiɣsan  n 
Yugurten. Yeccarrew. Yesferfed i weksum-is, iêukk iɣallen-is s 
ifassen-is  akken  ad  yesenɣes    tisuqqas  usemmiv-nni.  Tadyant-
nni  n  yizem  terna  deg-s  anezgum.  Yetkaki-d  imeddukal-is  n 
teméi. Gider, Ameqran, anida llan  ass-a ? 
Di  tesraft-nni,  izirig  arqaq  n  tafat  i  d-yudren  akin  si  tegnawt 
yebda  iselles.    Iéôa-nni  n  tesraft  i  as-d-yezzin  bdan  neṭlen 
yiwen yiwen.  Ur yefrin ma d ass i yeffalen akin i yiɣil am yal 
tameddit neɣ d iéri-s nepa i umi ddalent tillas, yebda yettderɣil. 
Yeqqen  aîîiwen-is,  yefka  tameééuɣt    ad  isel  i  wayen  i  as-d-
yezzin. Ur yella ûûut, ur yella wawal. Yuki i yiman-is yenîel d 
ameddur. Tuli-d tkuffirt deg-s, inteq ɣer yiman-is : 
-  "  Nekk,  Yugurten  n  At  Yiles,  aqli  di  tesraft  n  Ruma,    neîleɣ 
ddaw tmurt, ttwarzeɣ avar afus...". Di taɣect-is ur d yeffiɣ ûûut.

Yekref-d  tigecrar-is,  yesker 
iman-is  akken  ad  as-yenɣes 
usemmiv,  ma  d  allaɣ-is  yezger,  yunag  akin  i  yilel,  akin  i 
yidurar, akin i uzaɣar n tmurt-is. 
Yugurten  yerra  tamuɣli  ɣer  deffir,  ɣer  wussan  ineggura. 
Ussan-nni  tezzin  zdat  wallen-is,  tezzin  rennun  :  timlilit  n 
Tzaɣart, Buxuc, Sulla, Dabaô, Iôumaniyen zzin-as-d am wejôad, 
idammen, tisusaf, uzzal,  tixelxalin, yir awal... 
Yugurten yeîîef aqerruy-is ger ifassen-is, yewwet ad yekkes seg 
wallaɣ-is ayen akk iéeô di tedyant deg yella, taggara imukan n 
txelxalin-nni n wuzzal aéayan rrant-d tamuɣli-s ɣer wemkan-
nni  deg  yella.  Iêuk  iɣallen-is,  yuki  maççi  d  targit  i  yettargu. 
Yerna  yesself  i  yifassen-is,  i  yivaôôen-is,  ur  yeéôa  yella  neɣ  ur 
yella wuzzal-nni. 
Ayen  i  yesnedfen  ul-is  ugar  ur  yella  d  tadyant  yevran  yid-s, 
tufa-t-id ass-a yeîîef tama wadda zdat ucengu Aôumani. Tidet, 
nepa tuɣ-it yennum tilufa, yennum akessar d usawen, yennum 
uguren  seg  wass-mi  i  t-id-turew  yemma-s.  Isers  afus-is  ɣef 
yedmaren-is d tuyat-is, yesself i weksum-is, yuki i cwami-nni n 
tyitwin uneccab, tiyitwin ujenwi neɣ ucangal. £as llant cwami-
nni  deg  weksum-is,  ɣur-s  am  zun  ur  llant.  Acêal  imenɣiyen 
deg yella, deg yewwet, deg yeçça tiyita, taggara yufrar-d di yir 
tallit. Ajraê n tyita s ɣur ucengu yeqqaz iêellu... 
Ayen i yesnedfen ul-is ugar, d tiyita-nni i as-d-yekkan si deffir, 
seg yidammen-is. 
Yefka awal, yefka laman i  Buxuc akken  ad  yemlil nepa akk  d 
Sulla41.  Ad  mlilen  akken  ad  afen  tawwurt  n  tifrat  netta  akk  d 
Iôumaniyen,  Buxuc42  ad  yili  d  anagi.  Taggara  teffeɣ  tedyant 
akken nniven. 
Nekk ɣileɣ ad tili d timlilit n tifrat, d timlilit n Tzaɣart s ufus n 
Buxuc,  taggara  tuɣal  d  yir  targit.  Avewwal-is  yefka  afus  deg 
yidammen n warraw-is,  , yezzenz-it i Rruman. 
Akken  i  as-yewzen  Yugurten  ur  as-yufa  ixef-is.  Di  tazwara 
dduklen  netta  akk  d  Buxus,  sdukklen  tazmert-nsen  d  lâesker-

wadda am zun imir kan i d-nlul.

Ass-mi  llan  di  tattalt,  am  Aderbal  am  Hiemsal,  nekk  nudaɣ 
Tamazɣa  seg  yixef  ɣer  yixef,  seg  wagmud  ar  utaram,  seg 
wanéul ar ugafa. Zegreɣ isaffen, zegreɣ idurar, ulac tiɣremt ur 
kcimeɣ, ulac taddart ur ssineɣ. Anda kkiɣ d atmaten-iw, axxam 
kecmeɣ  d  axxam-iw.    Yal  tikkelt  s  mraw  ifassen  iyi-d-
ttmaggaren at tmurt-iw. 
Zegreɣ  ilel  ɣer  tmurt  n  Spanya,  kecmeɣ  di  ṭṭṛad  n  Numance, 
tama  n  lâesker  n  Rruman,  nemyefk  tayet,  neçça  aɣrum 
asemmav,  necrew  tidi  d  idammen.  Imir  Iôumaniyen  llan  d 
imeddukal-nneɣ, maççi am ass-nni am ass-a… 
Di Numance, isem n Tmazɣa yuli-as yiseɣ. 
Deg  imenɣi,  anda  terki,  anda  tegguma  ad  tefru  tyita,  d  nekk 
wuɣur d-idellu Scipion. Mi nekcem annar, ad neg afernas deg 
ucengu.  Dinna  di  Numance,  nesdukel  tamussni-nneɣ  di  ṭṭṛad 
akk  d  tin  nelmed  ɣer  Rruman.  Nerna-d  afud  i  yiseɣ  n 
yelmeéyen Imaziɣen i wwiɣ yid-i. Nefka ixef-nneɣ i wudem n 
yiseɣ n tmurt-nneɣ. 
Ass-mi  tefra  tin  n  Numance,  mi  nekker  ad  d-nuɣal,    zdat 
lâesker    d  yezzin  i  aɣ-d-yenna  Scipion  awalen  ineggura  : 
"kenwi  lâesker  n  Tmazɣa,  tefkam-aɣ-d  tayet,  tefkam  iqerray- 
nwen  i  tifrat  n  yimenɣi  n  Numance,  i  temɣer  n  Ruma. 

- 81 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Tzegrem-d  ilel  akken  ad  tegrem  afus  deg  yimenɣi  tama-nneɣ. 
Ass-a, azekka Ruma ur tettettu ayen tgam di tmurt dagi. ...". 
Neéra awal n Scipion  anda yessawev ass-a. 
Ass-mi d nuɣal si Numance, imeddukal-nneɣ yemmuten din ur 
ten-nettu.  Mi  d-nuɣal  kan,  nezzi-d  i  tmurt,  neéra  imawlan  n 
yergazen  i  neooa-n  akin  i  yilel.  D  lmut-nsen  i  yernan  azal  i 
tmurt n Tmazɣa ; iseɣ ameqqran, d yidammen-nsen nitni i t-id- 
yewwin i Makawsen." 
Tasusmi-nni  yedlen  Tullianum    terna-d  amur-is  n  tebrek  i 
tillas, i taéeyt uɣemɣum-nni. Idammen-nni sebken ɣef tuyat-is, 
rnan-d  tesmev  i  weksum-is.  Yugurten  yekna,  iger  afus-is  ad 
yennal  ixelxalen-nni  n  wuzzal  i  t-yurzen.  Yesferfed  ifassen 
ivaôôen ulac, ur llan ixelxalen-nni.  Yessarem ad ten-yaf akken 
ad ten-yeg d imwansen. 
Yuɣal-as i usaru-nni n tmeddurt is : 
"- Tiyita taneggarut n Buxuc, ɣas ukiɣ-as, s tidet tugar-itt tin d 
yekkan s ɣur watmaten-iw. Tiyita n Hiemsal, Aderbal, Masiwen 
akk d Gawda sfeclent-iyi. Terna-d tin n Bumelxir d timsislit. 
Anda  ilaq  tagmat  ad  tili  d  tagejdit  uɣur  ara  isenned  win 
yemdeôkalen, taggara yir tagmat terna-d aɣilif. 
Akka si zik, seg wass-mi tebda ddunit, tamurt-nneɣ ur as-tufa 
ixef-is. Si zik n zik, di yal tallit nekni neôwa akessar d usawen 
akken ad nesbedd tilisa n tmurt-nneɣ. Nezga-d ger sin icenga. 
Yiwet tama d Rruman, yiwet tama d Carthage i yegren tuccar- 
is di tmurt-nneɣ acêal iseggasen aya. 
I sin yid-sen skecmen-aɣ di tlufa yellan gar-asen. Tikkelt d wa, 
tikkelt  d  win.  ṭṭṛad  46  ameqqran  amezwaru  d-yellan  gar-asen  
acêal iseggasen aya, yekker ɣef tegzirt n Sisilya47. Ass-mi tefra 
gar-asen,  Rruman  iêella-d  Sisilya,  yerna-d  tigzirin  nniven, 
Sarda akk d Kursa.  
Carthage ur yella d tamurt s tidet. Carhage yusa-d am timmist 
deg weksum n Tamazɣa. Di tazwara-s d tiɣremt bnan Yefniqen 
zdat yillel Agrakal. Smeɣren akal-is s udegger n tlisa di tmurt-
nneɣ. Si tkemmict-nni n wakal n Tmazɣa akk d tmussni-nsen i

£as adabu-nsen nitni, amur ameqqran n yemnayen d ifellaêen-

Carthage  yeîîef    tamurt  n  Tmazɣa  s  ufus  d  tidi  n  tarwa  n 
Tmazɣa. Neɣɣ iman-nneɣ s ifassen-nneɣ ! 
Di  ṭṭṛad  wis  sin  i  ɣer  yekker  jedd-i  Masensen,  yefka  tayet  i 
Rruman, dduklen ɣef uqerruy n Carthage. 
Di tedyant-nni i d iban wudem n tidet n Tmazɣa : tamurt tebva 
ur  teddukel.  Di  yiwet  tama  d  Tamazɣa  (Numidya)  n  ugellid 
Masensen,  di  tama  nniven  d  Tamazɣa  (Muretanya)  n  ugellid 
Sifaks. 
Lemmer  dduklen  igelliden,  myefken  tayet,  yili  Carthage  ad 
yenger. Lemmer dduklen, Rruman  ad  yerr  avar,  ad  ikukru  ad 
d-yessekcem iman-is di tmurt-nneɣ. 
Akka i tella. Di ṭṭṛad wis sin, Masensen yedda d Rruman, Sifaks 
yedda  d  Carthage.  Tama  tekka  di  tayev.  Masensen  yekcem 
tiɣremt n Sirta, Sifaks icudd di snasel.  
Taɣennant-nni  yellan  gar  sin  igelliden,  anda  ilaq  da  teffer,  ad

nni  yellan  ger  Tmazɣa/Muretanya  akk  d  Tmazɣa/Numidya. 
Tamurt  yiwet,  laûel  yiwen,  iles  yiwen,  igelliden  tebva-ten 
tismin akk d tɣennant.

ass-a.  Beḍḍu  ger  Masensen  d  Sifaks  imir  yecba  beḍḍu  yellan 
taggara ger Yugurten akk Buxuc. £as akken  necrek idammen, 
tabaɛɛuct-nni n tɣennant d tismin n zik tekfel-d si ddaw tmurt, 
tessazzel idammen, tessawev-d Yugurten ɣer Tullianum..."

deg wallaɣ-is ilmend n tafat n tafukt ur iéeô.

tixeft, yevla s idammen.  D abrid n ṭṭṛad !    
Ger  wass  amezwaru  n  tikli  ugerram  d  wass  n  ṭṭṛad,  imir 
yezmer  ad  yili  webrid  n  tifrat  ger  Rruman  akk  d  yexûimen-
nsen.  Di yal tallit, ger ṭṭṛad d telwit, llan iberdan maççi yiwen.

abrid  n  telwit.  Anda  i  ten-tessawev  tezmert-nsen,  yiɣil-nsen,  i 
d-tekka  talast-nsen.  Azal  n  talast  ɣef  tebna  tmeddurt,  talast  n 
wakal, n wawal, n tikli, nitni ur tt-ssinen. Tga-yasen am tlafsa-
nni ur nessin tawat. 
Yella  deg  wawal  di  tmurt-nneɣ :  si  zik  n  zik,  talast  tella  ger 
wayen  yellan  d  wayen  ur  nella.  Tilisa  gan-tent  yemdanen 
akken  ad  beddent,  ad  ilint  gar-asen.  I  yal  talast  tella  tseɣlit-is. 
Tiseɣlit-nni  tella  kan  i  wallaɣ,  ur  tella  i  tezmert  ;  tella  kan 
akken  ad  yetkaki  wemdan  ansi  i  as-d-tegzem.  Dɣa,  ula  d 
izmawen  d  wuccayen  di  teégi  teggen  tilisa.  Yal  wa  deg 
wemviq-is.  £as  imdanen  ur  llan  d  uccanen  neɣ  d  izmawen,  si 
talast  ɣer  da  inek,  si  talast  akin  i  keçč.  Yal  yiwen  d  amur  n 
weɣbel-is.  Amkan  deg  ur  llant  tlisa,  d  nger  kan  i  ɣur-s  d-
iteddun. 
Ugur, maççi s ɣur Rruman kan i d-yusa.  Di tidet, tella deg-neɣ 
si zik n zik. Yella wayen yelhan, yella wayen n dir. Akka ! 
Iseggasen-agi ineggura deg necrew temreɣ, deg neôwa akessar 
d  usawen  deg  yimenɣiyen  d  lâeskeô  n  Rruman,  wwteɣ  ad  as-
afeɣ abrid-is, ad as-afeɣ ddwa, asafar ilaqen,  i wanda i tt-nuɣ.

Di ṭṭṛad, Iôumaniyen ur aɣ-ifen irgazen, ur aɣ-ugaren tirrugza,

tmurt !  
Di Numance51, di tmurt n Spanya, i d-sneɣ tamuɣli n Rruman, 
amek éeôôen tamurt-nsen, amek éeôôen timura n medden. Lliɣ 
meééiyeɣ,  maca  lliɣ  allen-iw,  sêeôceɣ  imeééuɣen-iw,  di  tallit-
nni n  umennuɣ di Numance mgal agellid Viriathe. 
Di  tlemmast  n  at  tmurt  i  tzemrev  ad  tissinev  at  tmurt-nni.  Di 
tlemmast  n  ṭṭṛad  i  tzemrev  a  tissinev  ugar  imdanen.  Di 
tlemmast n herwel, akken yella wemdan ara as-d-yefk udem-is, 
udem-nni  n  tidet.  Ur  yella  wurar,  ur  llant  tkerkas  ara  igen 
tagut i tidet. Di ḍḍiq, yal yiwen akken yella wudem-is i yella s 
timmad-is. Izem ad iban, awtul ur yezmir ad yentel. 
 
Abrid n Masensen. 
Ugur  ameqqran  yellan  gar-i  d  watmaten-iw,  Aderbal  akk  d 
Hiemsal, simmal yeééad deg wallaɣ-iw. Llant tikwal deg teggeɣ 
aɣilif Acku drus i d-yellan n awal, ur qqimeɣ ayen ilaqen akken 
ad  asen-sfeôzeɣ  ugar  abrid  éerreɣ,  abrid-nni-nwiɣ  ilaq  ad  t- 
nevfer.  Abrid-a  ur  yella  d  nekk  i  yeôéan  asalu-s.  Abrid-a  d 
abrid-nni n jedd-i, agellid Masensen. 
Abrid ɣas iban, tidet-is yevres, yeffer, tdel-it tagut n yiseggasen. 
Lemmer  yura  Jedd-i    Masensen  tamuɣli-s  d  wayen  yeḍran  di 
tgelda-s,    yili  yezmer  ahat  ur  aɣ-tverru  akka.  Mi  yedder 
Masensen,  mi  yemmut  Masensen,    awal-is,  ayen  yenna,  ayen 
iga,  ayen  iwehha,  nekni  nelqev-iten-id  d  iceqfan.    Lemmer 
yura  adlis  anda  d-yesefsi  tiyersiwin,  yili  ad  tifsus  fell-aɣ,  syin 
abrid ad aɣ-d-iban ɣer zdat. Yili daɣen nekk ad afeɣ tagest ɣef 
ara tekkiɣ. Ad afeɣ afud yes-s ara sdukleɣ atmaten-nneɣ i twizi 
tameqqrant. 
Tikwal,  mi  ara  d-tkakiɣ  tadyant  tamezwarut  i  aɣ-d-yeglan  s  
wuguren  imeqqranen  gar-aneɣ  seg-mi  yemmut  Makwasen, 
ttafeɣ  amur  ameqqran  seg  ɣur-neɣ  i  d-tekka.    Tilufa-nni  gar-

Di  tesraft-a  n  Tullianum  deg  lliɣ  ass-a,  ufiɣ  akken  tettulles

yefru irden s tiî-is. 
Seg wass-mi yekker Masensen, yekcem deg yimenɣiyen gar-as 
d Rruman akk d Carthage, tikwal yedda d wa, tikwal yedda d 
win,  tikli-s  di  tidet  yiwet  kan  i  yellan :  abrid-is  d  win  ara 
yesherwen Tamazɣa, seg yixef ɣer yixef, ad yekkes isem n tfidi 
n Cartage di Tmazɣa akken ad d tuɣal i Tmazɣa. Ma d Rruman 
ad yewwet akken ara yeqqim akin i yilel, akin di tmurt-is . 
Rruman  akk  d  Carthage  imir  jehden  i  sin,  myezmaren,  ma  d 
Tamazɣa  am  win  d  yekkren  d  ameéyan  ur  tseggem  tirkelt-is. 
Ilaq-as ad yernu tiram d iseggasen akken ad yefk afud i yiɣes-
is.  Aɣilif  ameqqran  d  beḍḍu-nni  tebva  Tmazɣa  ɣef  sin.  Yiwet 
tama  d  Masensen,  yiwet  tama  d  Sifaks.  Yal  wa  yekkat  ad 
yessemɣer iger-is s uhuddu n wayev, s uhuddu n gma-s !

yembawlen, yeccev, ad as-imal lkil.

yessemɣer iger n Ruma akin i yilel, akin i yidurar ; adrum-nni

Di  Carthage,  Hamilcar  Barca,  Asedrubal,  neɣ  Hannibal  kkren

Spanya,  rnan  tigzirin  n  Sarda  akk  d    Kursa.  Simmal  teddun, 
simmal sseqraben ɣer Ruma.

d  imenɣi  ameqqran52  gar-asen  nitni  d  Rruman.  Acêal  d 
aseggas, amennuɣ ur yefra. Tiɣmert deg tefra, ad d-tekker deg 
tayev.

annar.  Yal  yiwen  seg-sen,  Ruma  akk  d  Carthage,  yebɣa  ad

deg yimenɣi-s  mgal  axsim-is. Di tidet, yal yiwen  iswi-is  yebɣa 
ad  yekcem 
taggara-s  ɣef 
tamurt-nneɣ.  Urar-nsen  nitni, 
yiqerruyen-nneɣ. Tban am uzal !

ad yezwir deg wexsim amezwaru, Carthage, win i yuɣen aéar

uqerruy, ur tella telwit.

Yeqqumec di teɣmert, isenned ɣer sin yeéra akken ad yessenɣes 
tesmev  i  weksum-is.  Tikwal,  yif  teqreê  tesmev.  Udmawen  n

yeîîef. I d-yemmuger ufus-is ala ilem n tesraft. Nitni ur d-giren

- « Nuɣal i targit nekni nekni !  A wer nederwec !

neqqim.  Nnan  at  zik   « akken  triv  ɣezzifev  a  yiv,  taggara  ad 
yali wass ». 
Di  tmuɣli  n  tudert-nneɣ  nekni,  nesdukel  tudert  n  wid  yezrin, 
am zun yid-neɣ i llan, nerna tudert-nneɣ nekni akk d tudert n 
wid  d-iteddun  ɣer  zdat.  Di  yal  ass  ɣur-neɣ,  win  ibennun  ad 
yebnu, wid iteddun ɣer zdat, i warraw n warraw-is, ɣas netta 
di ḍḍiq i yella ; win  ileqqmen iteééun, ad yeééu isekla ara ççen 
wid  ara  d  yefôuôxen  ɣer  zdat,  ɣas  netta  ad  yezgel  tiram. 
Amedyaz,  win  yesefruyen  awal,  di  yal  tamurt,  awal-is  iteddu 
akin  i  wussan,  akin  i  yiseggasen  ɣer  zdat,  akken  awal-nni  ad 
yili d taftilt i webrid di tagut n tmeddurt.  Ma d avar yettôuéu 
asalu,  yezmer  ad  yefcel  neɣ  ad  yeâyu ;  awal  yeffal  akin  i  tizi, 
iteddu  irennu  tirkelt  i  tmussni.  Awal  ur  yezmir  yiwen  ad  t-
yeqqen, ur yezmir yiwen ad t-yekkes ma yuɣ timura, yeffeɣ am 
wavu, yuɣ idurar d izuɣar.

yal tiɣremt i kecmeɣ di Tmazɣa, di yal taddart i ɣer unfeɣ. 
Yiwen ur yezmir ad yekkes, ad yessenger awal-nni n tlelli.

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

Rruman ɣillen fran tadyant n Tmazɣa mi d-skecmen Yugurten 
deg tesraft-a n Tullianum.  Nekk ad sen-iniɣ, ur fran tigert. Ur 
yella  yiwen  Yugurten  kan  i  sen-d-yusan  d  asennan  deg 
weksum-nsen  i  Rruman.  Azekka,  yal  tiɣmert,  yal  tiɣilt,  yal 
azaɣar, yal tawrirt ad afen Yugurten ibedd-d zdat-nsen.  
Di  tikli-nni  n  Ruma,  mi  ériɣ  Marius  iteddu  ɣef  igemren 
imellalen,  s  ubeônus  azeggaɣ  ɣef  tuyat,  zdat-i  di  tlemmast  n 
Ruma, ériɣ-t am win ibedden akken ad yexbec igenni. Taéallit- 
is ur tessirid ammus  ameqqran, ammus ugertil58, ammus n yir 
iɣil, n yir tazmert. 
£urneɣ, tissas rennun i win yellan deg webrid n tissas. Ur llant 
tissas i win izegren ilel, yeréa tilisa n tmurt n medden, yekcem 
tamurt-nsen s uqeééul. 
Mi iyi-d-yeskecmen Iôumaniyen seg yimi n tesraft n 3 terdas di 
tehri, nitni ɣillen d anîal i neîlen Yugurten. Nwan kksen aɣilif-
nsen, wwven anda ssarmen. 
Nekk  ɣur-i,  anîar-nni  i  neîreɣ  seg  yimi  n  tesraft  ɣef  yeéra 
isemmaven, d talalit tis snat.  Am lufan-nni d-ilulen si tâebbuḍt 
n yemma-s s ibeddi, yezwer-d tiwuɣa. Nekk, awal-iw ooiɣ-t-in 
ɣer deffir i warraw n tmurt-nneɣ. Awal-iw yeffeɣ, yuɣ timura, 
yezger akin i tɣaltin, ur yezmir yiwen ad t-yarez. 
Azekka, aseggas, neɣ iseggasen d iseggasen ɣer zdat, ɣas awal- 
iw  yezmer  ad  yeffer,  ad  yenṭel  tallit  neɣ  ad  tdel  tagut  tallit, 
taggara  ad  yawev  wass  deg  ara  d-yefrari  i  tafat  n  tefsut,  ad 
yeddu, ad yennerni…

Tallit taneggarut 

 
 
 
 
 

 
 

Yugurten yemmut, deffir 6 wussan n laé d usemmiv. 

Ssuffɣen-t-id  si  tesraft-nni  n  Tullianum,  wwin-t  akin,    yeçça- 
wasif n Tiber, asif-nni yekkan di tlemmast n Rruman. 
Sin warraw n Yugurten i yellan ttwarzen yid-s, ur yeéra yiwen 
anda i d-gran.  Ur nessin ismawen-nsen, ur iban webrid uɣen 
asmi  tefra  tikli-nni  n  Ruma.  Yeɣba  yisem-nsen  si  tmurt  n 
Rruman. 
Yugurten  yemmut.  Ugur  ameqqran  deg  webrid-nsen,  nwan 
yekkes-asen i Rruman. Ufan abrid di tegnit, ééan tuééal-nsen di 
Tmazɣa.  Deffir  Yugurten,  snulfan-d  win  sbedden  d  agellid   i 
Tmazɣa : Gawda, gma-s n Yugurten s baba-s.  Rran-t d agellid 
am lexyal- nni n tebêirt akken ad kerzen yes-s. 
Nnan Gawda d abehlul kan, ur yessin,  ur yewzin, ur ixebbec 
ur iɣeé. Tamurt n Tmazɣa gezmen-tt, gezren-tt, gan-as iɣisan di 
tlemmast.  Amur  yefka-t  Rruman  i  ugellid  Buxuc,  rran-as  lxiô 
ilmend n tixubta-s, yezzenz idammen-is. 
Amur wis sin rnan-t nitni akken ad smeɣren tamurt n Carthage 
(province romaine). 
Tegra-d tiêdert n wakal, akk d tiɣremt n Sirta, yuɣal-as Gawda 
d agellid, ddaw ubeônus n Rruman ! Yuɣal d agellid ubeôwaq ! 
Taggara,  di  snat  turdas-nni  n  wakal  i  d  yegran  i  Gawda, 
yekcem  Uôumani  yal  taferka  yelhan,  yal  iger  yelhan,  yal 
tiɣremt. Tamurt tbeddel udem. 
Di tallit-nni, yeɣli-d yiv ɣef tmurt n Tmazɣa. Yeqqen uzaglu n 
Rruman i weɣref Amaziɣ.  Akken i teqqim ddeqs n leqrun…

- 105 : Calpurnius Bestia, Postumius Albinus, Cecilius Metellus, 
Caius Marius (yella yid-s Cornelius Sulla), 
 
-  105  : Cornelius  Sulla,  afesyan  yellan  ddaw  Marius,  yurez-d 
Yugurten. Icudd-it-id. Yezzenz-it i Rruman uvewwal-is Buxuc, 
agellid  n  Muriṭanya,  Tamazɣa  utaram  (Meôôuk  akk  d  umur 
ataram n Lezzayer), seg wasif n Melwen akin. 
 
-  105  (taggara) :  Marius  yezzuɣer-d  di  tlemmast  n  Ruma,  di 
tikli  n  "Triomphe",  Yugurten  akk  d  sin  warraw-is,  cudden  s 
txelxalin n wuzzal. 
 
 
 

- 95 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

- 104 (yennayer) : 
Yugurten yemmut di tesraft n Tullianum, deffir 6 wussan n laé, 
fad d usemmiv. Di leâmeô-is azal n 54 iseggasen. 
Gawda yuɣal d agellid n Tmazɣa, ddaw leânaya n Rruman. 
Sin warraw n Yugurten uckan ; ur yeéri yiwen anda i d-gran. 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

- 96 - 

 

- 7 - 
Amezruy n TULLIANUM 

 
 
 
 
 

 
 

Lêebs  Mamertine59  (Mamertinum  Carcere)  yella  di 
tlemmas n Ruma, tama n Capitole. Di tama n wadda n lêebs i 
tella tesraft Tullianum. 
Mamertinum  yebna-t  ugellid  Ancus  Marcius  di  lqern  wis  VII 
zdat Ɛisa. 
D  amkan  deg  anda  ttwarzen  yergazen,  anda  ttwaxenqen,  neɣ 
anda mmuten si laé icenga (yeâdawen) n Rruman. 
Ger  wid  yettwassnen,  wid  yemmuten  din,  yella  Yugurten  di 
yennayer -104, Vercingetorix, agellid n igulwaten (Fôansa),  
 

                                                            
59  «Ce  qui  reste  maintenant  du  Carcer  est  la  partie  la  plus  intérieure  et  la  plus 
secrète  du  cachot.  De 
l’église  S.  Giuseppe  dei  Falegnami  (St  Joseph  des 
Charpentiers),  un  escalier  moderne  conduit  à  l’édifice  antique  dont  la  façade  en 
travertin date du début de l’époque impériale. Derrière, on trouve une façade plus 
ancienne. La cellule supérieure de la prison est une pièce trapézoïdale, voûtée, de 5 
m sur 3 environ, reposant sur le roc, avec une hauteur de 5 m au point le plus élevé. 
La  cellule  inférieure,  le  Tullianum,  est  entièrement  construite  en  blocs  de  pépérin, 
assemblés  sans  mortier,  de  forme  conique,  avec  le  sommet  plat.  Dans  le  roc,  une 
ouverture de 70 cm (encore visible) la relie à la cellule supérieure. En l’absence de 
porte, c’est par ce trou que les condamnés étaient précipités. Sur le côté qui regarde 
le  Forum,  il  y  avait  un  égout  de  près  de  2  m  et  près  du  mur  opposé  à  l’égout,  un 
puits. Les blocs de tuf utilisés ici permettent d’avancer la date de la seconde moitié 
du IIe siècle av. J.-C. 
D’illustres personnages périrent ici – une inscription moderne gravée à droite de la 
porte d’entrée rappelle leur nom - comme Jugurtha, en 104 av. J.-C., pendant que 
défilait au Forum le cortège triomphal de son vainqueur, Marius. .. En 63 av. J.-C., 
les conjurés, amis de Catilina, y furent étranglés. En 46 av. J.-C., Vercingétorix y fut 
également étranglé après le triomphe de César. 
La  prison  ne  se  composait  pas  seulement  des  deux  cachots  décrits.  Au-delà,  sur  la 
pente du Capitole, se trouvaient d’autres pièces, les Lautumiae. Elle était encore en 
activité dans la dernière moitié du IVe siècle. C’est au Moyen-Age qu’elle prit le nom 
de Mamertine». 

- 97 - 

Tullianum, taggara n Yugurten 

i  umi 

semman 

tamesgida 

xenqen-t  din  deg  useggas  -46.  Ǧǧan-t  d  ameḥbus  14 
yiseggasen. Nnan daɣ, dinna i ttwarzen St Pierre akk d St Paul, 
asmi d-yekcem Ɛisa ɣer Ruma. 
Di  lqern  wis IV  deffir  Ɛisa,  lêebs-nni  hudden-t  si  tama  ufella, 
bnan-as 
"S.  Giuseppe  dei 
Falegnami"(Sidi Yusef n ineooaôen). 
Ayen  d  yegran  ass-a  di  lêebs  Mamertinum,    d  ayen  yellan  di 
tlemmast-is,  d  Tullianum-nni.  Akken  tella  tesraft-nni  zik-nni  i 
tella  ass-a,  bnan-as  kan  tiseddaôin  si  tama  akken  ad  adren 
medden ɣer tesraft, ad éuôen amkan-nni. Rnan ssan-as, sulin-d 
agens  d  asawen.  Si  3,53  m  n  tiddi,    gran-d  kan  2,0  m.  Ass-a, 
yezmer  ad  ibedd  wemdan  deg-s.  D  iéra-nni  n  zik,  d    iéra  n 
wass-a. 
 
Awal n Salluste ɣef Tullianum60 : 
 
"Mamertine  Carcere  d  lêebs  yellan  ddaw  tmurt,  deg-s  sin 
wannagen. Tama wadda d tasraft, isem-is Tullianum. Tedrem, 
yezzi-as-d ugadir, yeqba s weéru. Yiwen yimi  si tama ufella i d 
tawwurt-is, am zun d imi n wecbali. 
D amkan yexlan, yertem, yumes, yettulles, yessaggad." 
 
Abrid n tikli n Triomphe di Ruma. 
 
Tikli tedda si Campus Martius armi d Capitolus : 
(Abrid-is  di  tlemmast  n  teɣremt  n  Ruma,  tedda  seg  wennar 
Campus  Martius,  teffeɣ  ɣer  tewrirt  n  Capitolinus,  akken  ad 
yeééal dinna Consul ameqqran.) : 
- Campus Martius (Champ de Mars) 
- Circus Flaminus 
- Porte Triomphale (Pomerium) 
- Forum Boarium (>>ass-a isem-is «Piazza Bocca della verita») 
- Circus Maximus 

                                                            
60  C'était  une  prison  souterraine  à  deux  étages.  Selon  l'historien  Salluste  :  «  Elle 
contient une salle basse, nommée Tullianum, qui s'enfonce à douze pieds sous terre. 
Elle  est  fermée  de  murs  épais  et  couverte  d'une  voûte  de  pierre.  C'est  un  cachot 
malpropre,  obscur,  infect,  dont  l'aspect  a  quelque  chose  d'effrayant  et  d’horrible» 
(Salluste).
